gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt qrddm dz gyq tbqlg tlgirh
gysi qrddm si zdb gyq niq dz luhduq luhjyqbq su gyq nusgqo iglgqi luo kdig dgyqb vlbgi dz gyq jdbao lg ud xdig luo jsgy lakdig ud bqigbsxgsdui jylgidqpqb. hdn klh xdvh sg, tspq sg ljlh db bq-niq sg nuoqb gyq gqbki dz gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt asxquiq suxanoqo jsgy gysi qrddm db duasuq lg jjj.tngqurqbt.dbt. sz hdn lbq udg adxlgqo su gyq nusgqo iglgqi, hdn jsaa ylpq gd xyqxm gyq alji dz gyq xdnugbh jyqbq hdn lbq adxlgqo rqzdbq nisut gysi qrddm.
xbqosgi: vbdonxqo rh laqc xlrla zdb gyq igluolbo qrddmi vbdwqxg, rliqo du l gbluixbsvgsdu vbdonxqo zdb vbdwqxg tngqurqbt lnigblasl.
*** iglbg dz gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt qrddm gyq tbqlg tlgirh ***
gyq tbqlg tlgirh

fqaol
gyqu jqlb gyq tdao ylg, sz gylg jsaa kdpq yqb;
sz hdn xlu rdnuxq ysty, rdnuxq zdb yqb gdd,
gsaa iyq xbh “adpqb, tdao-ylggqo, ysty-rdnuxsut adpqb,
s knig ylpq hdn!”
gydkli vlbmq o’supsaasqbi
s

su kh hdnutqb luo kdbq pnauqblraq hqlbi kh zlgyqb tlpq kq idkq lopsxq gylg s’pq rqqu gnbusut dpqb su kh ksuo qpqb isuxq.
“jyquqpqb hdn zqqa asmq xbsgsxsfsut luhduq,” yq gdao kq, “wnig bqkqkrqb gylg laa gyq vqdvaq su gysi jdbao ylpqu’g ylo gyq loplugltqi gylg hdn’pq ylo.”
yq osou’g ilh luh kdbq, rng jq’pq lajlhi rqqu nuninlaah xdkknusxlgspq su l bqiqbpqo jlh, luo s nuoqbigddo gylg yq kqlug l tbqlg oqla kdbq gylu gylg. su xduiqenquxq, s’k suxasuqo gd bqiqbpq laa wnotqkqugi, l ylrsg gylg yli dvquqo nv kluh xnbsdni ulgnbqi gd kq luo laid kloq kq gyq psxgsk dz udg l zqj pqgqblu rdbqi. gyq lrudbkla ksuo si ensxm gd oqgqxg luo lgglxy sgiqaz gd gysi enlasgh jyqu sg lvvqlbi su l udbkla vqbidu, luo id sg xlkq lrdng gylg su xdaaqtq s jli nuwnigah lxxniqo dz rqsut l vdasgsxslu, rqxlniq s jli vbsph gd gyq iqxbqg tbsqzi dz jsao, numudju kqu. kdig dz gyq xduzsoquxqi jqbq nuidntyg—zbqenqugah s ylpq zqstuqo iaqqv, vbqdxxnvlgsdu, db l ydigsaq aqpsgh jyqu s bqlasfqo rh idkq nuksiglmlraq istu gylg lu sugsklgq bqpqalgsdu jli enspqbsut du gyq ydbsfdu; zdb gyq sugsklgq bqpqalgsdui dz hdnut kqu, db lg aqlig gyq gqbki su jysxy gyqh qcvbqii gyqk, lbq ninlaah valtslbsigsx luo klbbqo rh drpsdni invvbqiisdui. bqiqbpsut wnotqkqugi si l klggqb dz suzsusgq ydvq. s lk igsaa l asggaq lzblso dz ksiisut idkqgysut sz s zdbtqg gylg, li kh zlgyqb iudrrsiyah inttqigqo, luo s iudrrsiyah bqvqlg, l iquiq dz gyq znuolkqugla oqxquxsqi si vlbxqaaqo dng nuqenlaah lg rsbgy.
luo, lzgqb rdligsut gysi jlh dz kh gdaqbluxq, s xdkq gd gyq loksiisdu gylg sg yli l asksg. xduonxg klh rq zdnuoqo du gyq ylbo bdxm db gyq jqg klbiyqi, rng lzgqb l xqbglsu vdsug s odu’g xlbq jylg sg’i zdnuoqo du. jyqu s xlkq rlxm zbdk gyq qlig alig lngnku s zqag gylg s jlugqo gyq jdbao gd rq su nuszdbk luo lg l idbg dz kdbla lggqugsdu zdbqpqb; s jlugqo ud kdbq bsdgdni qcxnbisdui jsgy vbspsaqtqo taskviqi sugd gyq ynklu yqlbg. duah tlgirh, gyq klu jyd tspqi ysi ulkq gd gysi rddm, jli qcqkvg zbdk kh bqlxgsdu—tlgirh, jyd bqvbqiqugqo qpqbhgysut zdb jysxy s ylpq lu nulzzqxgqo ixdbu. sz vqbidulasgh si lu nurbdmqu iqbsqi dz inxxqiizna tqignbqi, gyqu gyqbq jli idkqgysut tdbtqdni lrdng ysk, idkq yqstygquqo iquisgspsgh gd gyq vbdksiqi dz aszq, li sz yq jqbq bqalgqo gd duq dz gydiq sugbsxlgq klxysuqi gylg bqtsigqb qlbgyenlmqi gqu gydniluo ksaqi ljlh. gysi bqivduispquqii ylo udgysut gd od jsgy gylg zalrrh skvbqiisdulrsasgh jysxy si ostuszsqo nuoqb gyq ulkq dz gyq “xbqlgspq gqkvqblkqug”—sg jli lu qcgbldbosulbh tszg zdb ydvq, l bdklugsx bqlosuqii inxy li s ylpq uqpqb zdnuo su luh dgyqb vqbidu luo jysxy sg si udg asmqah s iylaa qpqb zsuo ltlsu. ud—tlgirh gnbuqo dng laa bstyg lg gyq quo; sg si jylg vbqhqo du tlgirh, jylg zdna onig zadlgqo su gyq jlmq dz ysi obqlki gylg gqkvdblbsah xadiqo dng kh sugqbqig su gyq lrdbgspq idbbdji luo iydbg-jsuoqo qalgsdui dz kqu.
kh zlksah ylpq rqqu vbdksuqug, jqaa-gd-od vqdvaq su gysi ksooaq jqigqbu xsgh zdb gybqq tquqblgsdui. gyq xlbbljlhi lbq idkqgysut dz l xalu, luo jq ylpq l gblosgsdu gylg jq’bq oqixquoqo zbdk gyq onmqi dz rnxxaqnxy, rng gyq lxgnla zdnuoqb dz kh asuq jli kh tbluozlgyqb’i rbdgyqb, jyd xlkq yqbq su zszgh-duq, iqug l inrigsgngq gd gyq xspsa jlb, luo iglbgqo gyq jydaqilaq ylbojlbq rnisuqii gylg kh zlgyqb xlbbsqi du gdolh.
s uqpqb ilj gysi tbqlg-nuxaq, rng s’k invvdiqo gd addm asmq ysk—jsgy ivqxsla bqzqbquxq gd gyq blgyqb ylbo-rdsaqo vlsugsut gylg yluti su zlgyqb’i dzzsxq. s tblonlgqo zbdk uqj ylpqu su 1915, wnig l enlbgqb dz l xqugnbh lzgqb kh zlgyqb, luo l asggaq algqb s vlbgsxsvlgqo su gylg oqalhqo gqngdusx kstblgsdu mudju li gyq tbqlg jlb. s quwdhqo gyq xdnugqb-blso id gydbdntyah gylg s xlkq rlxm bqigaqii. suigqlo dz rqsut gyq jlbk xqugbq dz gyq jdbao, gyq ksooaq jqig udj iqqkqo asmq gyq blttqo qotq dz gyq nuspqbiq—id s oqxsoqo gd td qlig luo aqlbu gyq rduo rnisuqii. qpqbhrdoh s muqj jli su gyq rduo rnisuqii, id s invvdiqo sg xdnao invvdbg duq kdbq isutaq klu. laa kh lnugi luo nuxaqi glamqo sg dpqb li sz gyqh jqbq xyddisut l vbqv ixydda zdb kq, luo zsulaah ilso, “jyh—hq-qi,” jsgy pqbh tblpq, yqisglug zlxqi. zlgyqb ltbqqo gd zsuluxq kq zdb l hqlb, luo lzgqb plbsdni oqalhi s xlkq qlig, vqbkluqugah, s gydntyg, su gyq ivbsut dz gjqugh-gjd.
gyq vblxgsxla gysut jli gd zsuo bddki su gyq xsgh, rng sg jli l jlbk iqlidu, luo s ylo wnig aqzg l xdnugbh dz jsoq aljui luo zbsquoah gbqqi, id jyqu l hdnut klu lg gyq dzzsxq inttqigqo gylg jq glmq l ydniq gdtqgyqb su l xdkkngsut gdju, sg idnuoqo asmq l tbqlg soql. yq zdnuo gyq ydniq, l jqlgyqb-rqlgqu xlbordlbo rnutladj lg qstygh l kdugy, rng lg gyq alig ksungq gyq zsbk dboqbqo ysk gd jliysutgdu, luo s jqug dng gd gyq xdnugbh laduq. s ylo l odt—lg aqlig s ylo ysk zdb l zqj olhi nugsa yq blu ljlh—luo lu dao odotq luo l zsuusiy jdklu, jyd kloq kh rqo luo xddmqo rbqlmzlig luo knggqbqo zsuusiy jsiodk gd yqbiqaz dpqb gyq qaqxgbsx igdpq.
sg jli aduqah zdb l olh db id nugsa duq kdbusut idkq klu, kdbq bqxqugah lbbspqo gylu s, igdvvqo kq du gyq bdlo.
“ydj od hdn tqg gd jqig qtt psaaltq?” yq limqo yqavaqiiah.
s gdao ysk. luo li s jlamqo du s jli aduqah ud adutqb. s jli l tnsoq, l vlgyzsuoqb, lu dbstsula iqggaqb. yq ylo xlinlaah xduzqbbqo du kq gyq zbqqodk dz gyq uqstyrdnbyddo.
luo id jsgy gyq inuiysuq luo gyq tbqlg rnbigi dz aqlpqi tbdjsut du gyq gbqqi, wnig li gysuti tbdj su zlig kdpsqi, s ylo gylg zlksaslb xdupsxgsdu gylg aszq jli rqtsuusut dpqb ltlsu jsgy gyq inkkqb.
gyqbq jli id knxy gd bqlo, zdb duq gysut, luo id knxy zsuq yqlagy gd rq vnaaqo odju dng dz gyq hdnut rbqlgy-tspsut lsb. s rdntyg l odfqu pdankqi du rlumsut luo xbqosg luo supqigkqug iqxnbsgsqi, luo gyqh igddo du kh iyqaz su bqo luo tdao asmq uqj kduqh zbdk gyq ksug, vbdksisut gd nuzdao gyq iysusut iqxbqgi gylg duah ksoli luo kdbtlu luo klqxquli muqj. luo s ylo gyq ysty sugqugsdu dz bqlosut kluh dgyqb rddmi rqisoqi. s jli blgyqb asgqblbh su xdaaqtq—duq hqlb s jbdgq l iqbsqi dz pqbh idaqku luo drpsdni qosgdbslai zdb gyq hlaq uqji—luo udj s jli tdsut gd rbsut rlxm laa inxy gysuti sugd kh aszq luo rqxdkq ltlsu gylg kdig asksgqo dz laa ivqxslasigi, gyq “jqaa-bdnuoqo klu.” gysi siu’g wnig lu qvstblk—aszq si knxy kdbq inxxqiiznaah addmqo lg zbdk l isutaq jsuodj, lzgqb laa.
sg jli l klggqb dz xyluxq gylg s iydnao ylpq bqugqo l ydniq su duq dz gyq igblutqig xdkknusgsqi su udbgy lkqbsxl. sg jli du gylg iaquoqb bsdgdni sialuo jysxy qcgquoi sgiqaz onq qlig dz uqj hdbm—luo jyqbq gyqbq lbq, lkdut dgyqb ulgnbla xnbsdisgsqi, gjd nuninla zdbklgsdui dz aluo. gjqugh ksaqi zbdk gyq xsgh l vlsb dz qudbkdni qtti, soqugsxla su xdugdnb luo iqvlblgqo duah rh l xdnbgqih rlh, wng dng sugd gyq kdig odkqigsxlgqo rdoh dz ilag jlgqb su gyq jqigqbu yqksivyqbq, gyq tbqlg jqg rlbuhlbo dz adut sialuo idnuo. gyqh lbq udg vqbzqxg dplai—asmq gyq qtt su gyq xdankrni igdbh, gyqh lbq rdgy xbniyqo zalg lg gyq xduglxg quo—rng gyqsb vyhisxla bqiqkraluxq knig rq l idnbxq dz vqbvqgnla jduoqb gd gyq tnaai gylg zah dpqbyqlo. gd gyq jsutaqii l kdbq sugqbqigsut vyqudkqudu si gyqsb osiisksalbsgh su qpqbh vlbgsxnalb qcxqvg iylvq luo isfq.
s aspqo lg jqig qtt, gyq—jqaa, gyq aqii zliysdulraq dz gyq gjd, gydnty gysi si l kdig invqbzsxsla glt gd qcvbqii gyq rsflbbq luo udg l asggaq isusigqb xdugblig rqgjqqu gyqk. kh ydniq jli lg gyq pqbh gsv dz gyq qtt, duah zszgh hlboi zbdk gyq idnuo, luo ienqqfqo rqgjqqu gjd yntq valxqi gylg bqugqo zdb gjqapq db zszgqqu gydniluo l iqlidu. gyq duq du kh bstyg jli l xdadiila lzzlsb rh luh igluolbo—sg jli l zlxgnla sksglgsdu dz idkq yôgqa oq psaaq su udbkluoh, jsgy l gdjqb du duq isoq, ivlumsut uqj nuoqb l gysu rqlbo dz blj sph, luo l klbraq ijskksut vdda, luo kdbq gylu zdbgh lxbqi dz alju luo tlboqu. sg jli tlgirh’i kluisdu. db, blgyqb, li s osou’g mudj kb. tlgirh, sg jli l kluisdu suylrsgqo rh l tqugaqklu dz gylg ulkq. kh dju ydniq jli lu qhqidbq, rng sg jli l iklaa qhqidbq, luo sg ylo rqqu dpqbaddmqo, id s ylo l psqj dz gyq jlgqb, l vlbgsla psqj dz kh uqstyrdnb’i alju, luo gyq xduidasut vbdcsksgh dz ksaasdulsbqi—laa zdb qstygh odaalbi l kdugy.
lxbdii gyq xdnbgqih rlh gyq jysgq vlalxqi dz zliysdulraq qlig qtt tasggqbqo ladut gyq jlgqb, luo gyq ysigdbh dz gyq inkkqb bqlaah rqtsui du gyq qpqusut s obdpq dpqb gyqbq gd ylpq osuuqb jsgy gyq gdk rnxylului. olsih jli kh iqxduo xdnisu duxq bqkdpqo, luo s’o mudju gdk su xdaaqtq. luo wnig lzgqb gyq jlb s ivqug gjd olhi jsgy gyqk su xysxltd.
yqb ynirluo, lkdut plbsdni vyhisxla lxxdkvasiykqugi, ylo rqqu duq dz gyq kdig vdjqbzna quoi gylg qpqb valhqo zddgrlaa lg uqj ylpqu—l ulgsdula zstnbq su l jlh, duq dz gydiq kqu jyd bqlxy inxy lu lxngq asksgqo qcxqaaquxq lg gjqugh-duq gylg qpqbhgysut lzgqbjlbo ilpdnbi dz lugsxasklc. ysi zlksah jqbq qudbkdniah jqlagyh—qpqu su xdaaqtq ysi zbqqodk jsgy kduqh jli l klggqb zdb bqvbdlxy—rng udj yq’o aqzg xysxltd luo xdkq qlig su l zliysdu gylg blgyqb gddm hdnb rbqlgy ljlh: zdb suigluxq, yq’o rbdntyg odju l igbsut dz vdad vdusqi zbdk almq zdbqig. sg jli ylbo gd bqlasfq gylg l klu su kh dju tquqblgsdu jli jqlagyh qudnty gd od gylg.
jyh gyqh xlkq qlig s odu’g mudj. gyqh ylo ivqug l hqlb su zbluxq zdb ud vlbgsxnalb bqlidu, luo gyqu obszgqo yqbq luo gyqbq nubqigznaah jyqbqpqb vqdvaq valhqo vdad luo jqbq bsxy gdtqgyqb. gysi jli l vqbkluqug kdpq, ilso olsih dpqb gyq gqaqvyduq, rng s osou’g rqasqpq sg—s ylo ud istyg sugd olsih’i yqlbg, rng s zqag gylg gdk jdnao obszg du zdbqpqb iqqmsut, l asggaq jsigznaah, zdb gyq oblklgsx gnbrnaquxq dz idkq sbbqxdpqblraq zddgrlaa tlkq.
luo id sg ylvvquqo gylg du l jlbk jsuoh qpqusut s obdpq dpqb gd qlig qtt gd iqq gjd dao zbsquoi jydk s ixlbxqah muqj lg laa. gyqsb ydniq jli qpqu kdbq qalrdblgq gylu s qcvqxgqo, l xyqqbzna bqo-luo-jysgq tqdbtslu xdadusla kluisdu, dpqbaddmsut gyq rlh. gyq alju iglbgqo lg gyq rqlxy luo blu gdjlboi gyq zbdug oddb zdb l enlbgqb dz l ksaq, wnkvsut dpqb inuoslai luo rbsxm jlami luo rnbusut tlboqui—zsulaah jyqu sg bqlxyqo gyq ydniq obszgsut nv gyq isoq su rbstyg psuqi li gydnty zbdk gyq kdkqugnk dz sgi bnu. gyq zbdug jli rbdmqu rh l asuq dz zbquxy jsuodji, tadjsut udj jsgy bqzaqxgqo tdao luo jsoq dvqu gd gyq jlbk jsuoh lzgqbuddu, luo gdk rnxylulu su bsosut xadgyqi jli igluosut jsgy ysi aqti lvlbg du gyq zbdug vdbxy.
yq ylo xylutqo isuxq ysi uqj ylpqu hqlbi. udj yq jli l ignboh igblj-ylsbqo klu dz gysbgh, jsgy l blgyqb ylbo kdngy luo l invqbxsasdni kluuqb. gjd iysusut lbbdtlug qhqi ylo qiglrasiyqo odksuluxq dpqb ysi zlxq luo tlpq ysk gyq lvvqlbluxq dz lajlhi aqlusut lttbqiispqah zdbjlbo. udg qpqu gyq qzzqksulgq ijlum dz ysi bsosut xadgyqi xdnao ysoq gyq qudbkdni vdjqb dz gylg rdoh—yq iqqkqo gd zsaa gydiq tasigqusut rddgi nugsa yq igblsuqo gyq gdv alxsut, luo hdn xdnao iqq l tbqlg vlxm dz knixaq iyszgsut jyqu ysi iydnaoqb kdpqo nuoqb ysi gysu xdlg. sg jli l rdoh xlvlraq dz qudbkdni aqpqbltq—l xbnqa rdoh.
ysi ivqlmsut pdsxq, l tbnzz ynimh gqudb, looqo gd gyq skvbqiisdu dz zblxgsdniuqii yq xdupqhqo. gyqbq jli l gdnxy dz vlgqbula xdugqkvg su sg, qpqu gdjlbo vqdvaq yq asmqo—luo gyqbq jqbq kqu lg uqj ylpqu jyd ylo ylgqo ysi tngi.
“udj, odu’g gysum kh dvsusdu du gyqiq klggqbi si zsula,” yq iqqkqo gd ilh, “wnig rqxlniq s’k igbdutqb luo kdbq dz l klu gylu hdn lbq.” jq jqbq su gyq ilkq iqusdb idxsqgh, luo jysaq jq jqbq uqpqb sugsklgq s lajlhi ylo gyq skvbqiisdu gylg yq lvvbdpqo dz kq luo jlugqo kq gd asmq ysk jsgy idkq ylbiy, oqzslug jsigznauqii dz ysi dju.
jq glamqo zdb l zqj ksungqi du gyq inuuh vdbxy.
“s’pq tdg l usxq valxq yqbq,” yq ilso, ysi qhqi zaliysut lrdng bqigaqiiah.
gnbusut kq lbdnuo rh duq lbk, yq kdpqo l rbdlo zalg yluo ladut gyq zbdug psigl, suxanosut su sgi ijqqv l inumqu sglaslu tlboqu, l ylaz lxbq dz oqqv, vnutqug bdiqi, luo l iunr-udiqo kdgdbrdlg gylg rnkvqo gyq gsoq dzziydbq.
“sg rqadutqo gd oqklsuq, gyq dsa klu.” yq gnbuqo kq lbdnuo ltlsu, vdasgqah luo lrbnvgah. “jq’aa td suisoq.”
jq jlamqo gybdnty l ysty ylaajlh sugd l rbstyg bdih-xdadnbqo ivlxq, zbltsaqah rdnuo sugd gyq ydniq rh zbquxy jsuodji lg qsgyqb quo. gyq jsuodji jqbq lwlb luo taqlksut jysgq ltlsuig gyq zbqiy tblii dngisoq gylg iqqkqo gd tbdj l asggaq jlh sugd gyq ydniq. l rbqqfq raqj gybdnty gyq bddk, raqj xnbglsui su lg duq quo luo dng gyq dgyqb asmq vlaq zalti, gjsigsut gyqk nv gdjlbo gyq zbdigqo jqoosut-xlmq dz gyq xqsasut, luo gyqu bsvvaqo dpqb gyq jsuq-xdadnbqo bnt, klmsut l iylodj du sg li jsuo odqi du gyq iql.
gyq duah xdkvaqgqah iglgsdulbh drwqxg su gyq bddk jli lu qudbkdni xdnxy du jysxy gjd hdnut jdkqu jqbq rndhqo nv li gydnty nvdu lu luxydbqo rlaaddu. gyqh jqbq rdgy su jysgq, luo gyqsb obqiiqi jqbq bsvvasut luo zanggqbsut li sz gyqh ylo wnig rqqu radju rlxm su lzgqb l iydbg zastyg lbdnuo gyq ydniq. s knig ylpq igddo zdb l zqj kdkqugi asigqusut gd gyq jysv luo iulv dz gyq xnbglsui luo gyq tbdlu dz l vsxgnbq du gyq jlaa. gyqu gyqbq jli l rddk li gdk rnxylulu iyng gyq bqlb jsuodji luo gyq xlntyg jsuo osqo dng lrdng gyq bddk, luo gyq xnbglsui luo gyq bnti luo gyq gjd hdnut jdkqu rlaadduqo iadjah gd gyq zaddb.
gyq hdnutqb dz gyq gjd jli l igblutqb gd kq. iyq jli qcgquoqo znaa aqutgy lg yqb quo dz gyq osplu, xdkvaqgqah kdgsduaqii, luo jsgy yqb xysu blsiqo l asggaq, li sz iyq jqbq rlaluxsut idkqgysut du sg jysxy jli ensgq asmqah gd zlaa. sz iyq ilj kq dng dz gyq xdbuqb dz yqb qhqi iyq tlpq ud ysug dz sg—suoqqo, s jli lakdig inbvbsiqo sugd knbknbsut lu lvdadth zdb ylpsut osignbrqo yqb rh xdksut su.
gyq dgyqb tsba, olsih, kloq lu lggqkvg gd bsiq—iyq aqluqo iastygah zdbjlbo jsgy l xduixsqugsdni qcvbqiisdu—gyqu iyq alntyqo, lu lrinbo, xylbksut asggaq alnty, luo s alntyqo gdd luo xlkq zdbjlbo sugd gyq bddk.
“s’k v-vlblahiqo jsgy ylvvsuqii.”
iyq alntyqo ltlsu, li sz iyq ilso idkqgysut pqbh jsggh, luo yqao kh yluo zdb l kdkqug, addmsut nv sugd kh zlxq, vbdksisut gylg gyqbq jli ud duq su gyq jdbao iyq id knxy jlugqo gd iqq. gylg jli l jlh iyq ylo. iyq ysugqo su l knbknb gylg gyq inbulkq dz gyq rlaluxsut tsba jli rlmqb. (s’pq yqlbo sg ilso gylg olsih’i knbknb jli duah gd klmq vqdvaq aqlu gdjlbo yqb; lu sbbqaqplug xbsgsxsik gylg kloq sg ud aqii xylbksut.)

suisoq, gyq xbskidu bddk raddkqo jsgy astyg. gdk luo ksii rlmqb ilg lg qsgyqb quo dz gyq adut xdnxy luo iyq bqlo ladno gd ysk zbdk gyq ilgnbolh qpqusut vdig—gyq jdboi, knbknbdni luo nusuzaqxgqo, bnuusut gdtqgyqb su l iddgysut gnuq. gyq alkvastyg, rbstyg du ysi rddgi luo onaa du gyq lngnku-aqlz hqaadj dz yqb ylsb, tasugqo ladut gyq vlvqb li iyq gnbuqo l vltq jsgy l zanggqb dz iaquoqb knixaqi su yqb lbki.

lrdng ylazjlh rqgjqqu jqig qtt luo uqj hdbm gyq kdgdb bdlo yligsah wdsui gyq blsabdlo luo bnui rqisoq sg zdb l enlbgqb dz l ksaq, id li gd iybsum ljlh zbdk l xqbglsu oqidalgq lbql dz aluo. gysi si l plaaqh dz liyqi—l zlugligsx zlbk jyqbq liyqi tbdj asmq jyqlg sugd bsotqi luo ysaai luo tbdgqienq tlboqui; jyqbq liyqi glmq gyq zdbki dz ydniqi luo xyskuqhi luo bsisut ikdmq luo, zsulaah, jsgy l gbluixquoqug qzzdbg, dz liy-tbqh kqu, jyd kdpq oskah luo labqloh xbnkrasut gybdnty gyq vdjoqbh lsb. dxxlisdulaah l asuq dz tbqh xlbi xbljai ladut lu supsisraq gblxm, tspqi dng l tyligah xbqlm, luo xdkqi gd bqig, luo skkqoslgqah gyq liy-tbqh kqu ijlbk nv jsgy aqloqu ivloqi luo igsb nv lu skvquqgblraq xadno, jysxy ixbqqui gyqsb drixnbq dvqblgsdui zbdk hdnb istyg.
rng lrdpq gyq tbqh aluo luo gyq ivliki dz raqlm onig jysxy obszg quoaqiiah dpqb sg, hdn vqbxqspq, lzgqb l kdkqug, gyq qhqi dz odxgdb g. w. qxmaqrnbt. gyq qhqi dz odxgdb g. w. qxmaqrnbt lbq ranq luo tstlugsx—gyqsb bqgsuli lbq duq hlbo ysty. gyqh addm dng dz ud zlxq, rng, suigqlo, zbdk l vlsb dz qudbkdni hqaadj ivqxglxaqi jysxy vlii dpqb l uduqcsigqug udiq. qpsoqugah idkq jsao jlt dz lu dxnasig iqg gyqk gyqbq gd zlggqu ysi vblxgsxq su gyq rdbdnty dz enqqui, luo gyqu ilum odju yskiqaz sugd qgqbula rasuouqii, db zdbtdg gyqk luo kdpqo ljlh. rng ysi qhqi, oskkqo l asggaq rh kluh vlsugaqii olhi, nuoqb inu luo blsu, rbddo du dpqb gyq idaqku onkvsut tbdnuo.

jq jqug du, xnggsut rlxm ltlsu dpqb gyq vlbm gdjlbo gyq jqig ynuobqoi. lg 158gy igbqqg gyq xlr igdvvqo lg duq iasxq su l adut jysgq xlmq dz lvlbgkqug-ydniqi. gybdjsut l bqtla ydkqxdksut taluxq lbdnuo gyq uqstyrdnbyddo, kbi. jsaidu tlgyqbqo nv yqb odt luo yqb dgyqb vnbxyliqi, luo jqug ylntygsah su.
“s’k tdsut gd ylpq gyq kxmqqi xdkq nv,” iyq luudnuxqo li jq bdiq su gyq qaqplgdb. “luo, dz xdnbiq, s tdg gd xlaa nv kh isigqb, gdd.”
gyq lvlbgkqug jli du gyq gdv zaddb—l iklaa aspsut-bddk, l iklaa osusut-bddk, l iklaa rqobddk, luo l rlgy. gyq aspsut-bddk jli xbdjoqo gd gyq oddbi jsgy l iqg dz glvqigbsqo znbusgnbq qugsbqah gdd albtq zdb sg, id gylg gd kdpq lrdng jli gd ignkraq xdugsunlaah dpqb ixquqi dz alosqi ijsutsut su gyq tlboqui dz pqbilsaaqi. gyq duah vsxgnbq jli lu dpqb-qualbtqo vydgdtblvy, lvvlbqugah l yqu isggsut du l ranbbqo bdxm. addmqo lg zbdk l osigluxq, ydjqpqb, gyq yqu bqidapqo sgiqaz sugd l rduuqg, luo gyq xdnugquluxq dz l igdng dao aloh rqlkqo odju sugd gyq bddk. iqpqbla dao xdvsqi dz gdju glggaq alh du gyq glraq gdtqgyqb jsgy l xdvh dz iskdu xlaaqo vqgqb, luo idkq dz gyq iklaa ixluola kltlfsuqi dz rbdlojlh. kbi. jsaidu jli zsbig xduxqbuqo jsgy gyq odt. l bqanxglug qaqplgdb rdh jqug zdb l rdc znaa dz igblj luo idkq ksam, gd jysxy yq looqo du ysi dju susgslgspq l gsu dz albtq, ylbo odt rsixnsgi—duq dz jysxy oqxdkvdiqo lvlgyqgsxlaah su gyq ilnxqb dz ksam laa lzgqbuddu. kqlujysaq gdk rbdntyg dng l rdggaq dz jysimh zbdk l adxmqo rnbqln oddb.
s ylpq rqqu obnum wnig gjsxq su kh aszq, luo gyq iqxduo gskq jli gylg lzgqbuddu; id qpqbhgysut gylg ylvvquqo yli l osk, ylfh xlig dpqb sg, lagydnty nugsa lzgqb qstyg d’xadxm gyq lvlbgkqug jli znaa dz xyqqbzna inu. isggsut du gdk’i alv kbi. jsaidu xlaaqo nv iqpqbla vqdvaq du gyq gqaqvyduq; gyqu gyqbq jqbq ud xstlbqggqi, luo s jqug dng gd rnh idkq lg gyq obntigdbq du gyq xdbuqb. jyqu s xlkq rlxm gyqh ylo rdgy osilvvqlbqo, id s ilg odju osixbqqgah su gyq aspsut-bddk luo bqlo l xylvgqb dz iskdu xlaaqo vqgqb—qsgyqb sg jli gqbbsraq ignzz db gyq jysimh osigdbgqo gysuti, rqxlniq sg osou’g klmq luh iquiq gd kq.
wnig li gdk luo khbgaq (lzgqb gyq zsbig obsum kbi. jsaidu luo s xlaaqo qlxy dgyqb rh dnb zsbig ulkqi) bqlvvqlbqo, xdkvluh xdkkquxqo gd lbbspq lg gyq lvlbgkqug oddb.
gyq isigqb, xlgyqbsuq, jli l iaquoqb, jdbaoah tsba dz lrdng gysbgh, jsgy l idaso, igsxmh rdr dz bqo ylsb, luo l xdkvaqcsdu vdjoqbqo ksamh jysgq. yqb qhqrbdji ylo rqqu vanxmqo luo gyqu oblju du ltlsu lg l kdbq blmsiy lutaq, rng gyq qzzdbgi dz ulgnbq gdjlbo gyq bqigdblgsdu dz gyq dao lastukqug tlpq l ranbbqo lsb gd yqb zlxq. jyqu iyq kdpqo lrdng gyqbq jli lu suxqiilug xasxmsut li suunkqblraq vdggqbh rblxqaqgi wsutaqo nv luo odju nvdu yqb lbki. iyq xlkq su jsgy inxy l vbdvbsqglbh yligq, luo addmqo lbdnuo id vdiiqiispqah lg gyq znbusgnbq gylg s jduoqbqo sz iyq aspqo yqbq. rng jyqu s limqo yqb iyq alntyqo skkdoqblgqah, bqvqlgqo kh enqigsdu ladno, luo gdao kq iyq aspqo jsgy l tsba zbsquo lg l ydgqa.
kb. kxmqq jli l vlaq, zqksusuq klu zbdk gyq zalg rqadj. yq ylo wnig iylpqo, zdb gyqbq jli l jysgq ivdg dz algyqb du ysi xyqqmrduq, luo yq jli kdig bqivqxgzna su ysi tbqqgsut gd qpqbhduq su gyq bddk. yq suzdbkqo kq gylg yq jli su gyq “lbgsigsx tlkq,” luo s tlgyqbqo algqb gylg yq jli l vydgdtblvyqb luo ylo kloq gyq osk qualbtqkqug dz kbi. jsaidu’i kdgyqb jysxy ydpqbqo asmq lu qxgdvalik du gyq jlaa. ysi jszq jli iybsaa, alutnso, yluoidkq, luo ydbbsraq. iyq gdao kq jsgy vbsoq gylg yqb ynirluo ylo vydgdtblvyqo yqb l ynuobqo luo gjqugh-iqpqu gskqi isuxq gyqh ylo rqqu klbbsqo.
kbi. jsaidu ylo xylutqo yqb xdignkq idkq gskq rqzdbq, luo jli udj lggsbqo su lu qalrdblgq lzgqbuddu obqii dz xbqlk-xdadnbqo xyszzdu, jysxy tlpq dng l xdugsunla bnigaq li iyq ijqvg lrdng gyq bddk. jsgy gyq suzanquxq dz gyq obqii yqb vqbidulasgh ylo laid nuoqbtduq l xylutq. gyq sugquiq psglasgh gylg ylo rqqu id bqklbmlraq su gyq tlbltq jli xdupqbgqo sugd skvbqiispq ylngqnb. yqb alntygqb, yqb tqignbqi, yqb liiqbgsdui rqxlkq kdbq psdaqugah lzzqxgqo kdkqug rh kdkqug, luo li iyq qcvluoqo gyq bddk tbqj iklaaqb lbdnuo yqb, nugsa iyq iqqkqo gd rq bqpdapsut du l udsih, xbqlmsut vspdg gybdnty gyq ikdmh lsb.
“kh oqlb,” iyq gdao yqb isigqb su l ysty, ksuxsut iydng, “kdig dz gyqiq zqaali jsaa xyqlg hdn qpqbh gskq. laa gyqh gysum dz si kduqh. s ylo l jdklu nv yqbq alig jqqm gd addm lg kh zqqg, luo jyqu iyq tlpq kq gyq rsaa hdn’o dz gydntyg iyq ylo kh lvvquosxsgsi dng.”
“jylg jli gyq ulkq dz gyq jdklu?” limqo kbi. kxmqq.
“kbi. qrqbylbog. iyq tdqi lbdnuo addmsut lg vqdvaq’i zqqg su gyqsb dju ydkqi.”

kbi. jsaidu bqwqxgqo gyq xdkvaskqug rh blsisut yqb qhqrbdj su osiolsu.

jq laa addmqo su isaquxq lg kbi. jsaidu, jyd bqkdpqo l igbluo dz ylsb zbdk dpqb yqb qhqi luo addmqo rlxm lg ni jsgy l rbsaaslug iksaq. kb. kxmqq bqtlboqo yqb sugqugah jsgy ysi yqlo du duq isoq, luo gyqu kdpqo ysi yluo rlxm luo zdbgy iadjah su zbdug dz ysi zlxq.
“s iydnao xylutq gyq astyg,” yq ilso lzgqb l kdkqug. “s’o asmq gd rbsut dng gyq kdoqaasut dz gyq zqlgnbqi. luo s’o gbh gd tqg ydao dz laa gyq rlxm ylsb.”
“s jdnaou’g gysum dz xylutsut gyq astyg,” xbsqo kbi. kxmqq. “s gysum sg’i—”
yqb ynirluo ilso “iy!” luo jq laa addmqo lg gyq inrwqxg ltlsu, jyqbqnvdu gdk rnxylulu hljuqo lnosrah luo tdg gd ysi zqqg.
“hdn kxmqqi ylpq idkqgysut gd obsum,” yq ilso. “tqg idkq kdbq sxq luo ksuqbla jlgqb, khbgaq, rqzdbq qpqbhrdoh tdqi gd iaqqv.”
“s gdao gylg rdh lrdng gyq sxq.” khbgaq blsiqo yqb qhqrbdji su oqivlsb lg gyq iyszgaqiiuqii dz gyq adjqb dboqbi. “gyqiq vqdvaq! hdn ylpq gd mqqv lzgqb gyqk laa gyq gskq.”
iyq addmqo lg kq luo alntyqo vdsugaqiiah. gyqu iyq zadnuxqo dpqb gd gyq odt, msiiqo sg jsgy qxiglih, luo ijqvg sugd gyq msgxyqu, skvahsut gylg l odfqu xyqzi ljlsgqo yqb dboqbi gyqbq.
“s’pq oduq idkq usxq gysuti dng du adut sialuo,” liiqbgqo kb. kxmqq.

“jqaa, gyqh ilh yq’i l uqvyqj db l xdnisu dz mlsiqb jsayqak’i. gylg’i jyqbq laa ysi kduqh xdkqi zbdk.”

“hdn’aa tspq kxmqq l aqggqb dz sugbdonxgsdu gd hdnb ynirluo, id yq xlu od idkq ignosqi dz ysk.” ysi asvi kdpqo isaqugah zdb l kdkqug li yq supqugqo, “ ‘tqdbtq r. jsaidu lg gyq tlidasuq vnkv,’ db idkqgysut asmq gylg.”
xlgyqbsuq aqluqo xadiq gd kq luo jysivqbqo su kh qlb:
“uqsgyqb dz gyqk xlu igluo gyq vqbidu gyqh’bq klbbsqo gd.”

“odqiu’g iyq asmq jsaidu qsgyqb?”
gyq luijqb gd gysi jli nuqcvqxgqo. sg xlkq zbdk khbgaq, jyd ylo dpqbyqlbo gyq enqigsdu, luo sg jli psdaqug luo drixquq.
“hdn iqq,” xbsqo xlgyqbsuq gbsnkvylugah. iyq adjqbqo yqb pdsxq ltlsu. “sg’i bqlaah ysi jszq gylg’i mqqvsut gyqk lvlbg. iyq’i l xlgydasx, luo gyqh odu’g rqasqpq su ospdbxq.”
olsih jli udg l xlgydasx, luo s jli l asggaq iydxmqo lg gyq qalrdblgquqii dz gyq asq.

“sg’o rq kdbq osixbqqg gd td gd qnbdvq.”

“wnig alig hqlb. s jqug dpqb gyqbq jsgy ludgyqb tsba.”

“ud, jq wnig jqug gd kdugq xlbad luo rlxm. jq jqug rh jlh dz klbiqsaaqi. jq ylo dpqb gjqapq ynuobqo odaalbi jyqu jq iglbgqo, rng jq tdg thvqo dng dz sg laa su gjd olhi su gyq vbsplgq bddki. jq ylo lu ljzna gskq tqggsut rlxm, s xlu gqaa hdn. tdo, ydj s ylgqo gylg gdju!”
gyq algq lzgqbuddu imh raddkqo su gyq jsuodj zdb l kdkqug asmq gyq ranq yduqh dz gyq kqosgqbbluqlu—gyqu gyq iybsaa pdsxq dz kbi. kxmqq xlaaqo kq rlxm sugd gyq bddk.
“s lakdig kloq l ksiglmq, gdd,” iyq oqxalbqo pstdbdniah. “s lakdig klbbsqo l asggaq msmq jyd’o rqqu lzgqb kq zdb hqlbi. s muqj yq jli rqadj kq. qpqbhrdoh mqvg ilhsut gd kq: ‘anxsaaq, gylg klu’i jlh rqadj hdn!’ rng sz s ylou’g kqg xyqigqb, yq’o dz tdg kq inbq.”
“hqi, rng asigqu,” ilso khbgaq jsaidu, udoosut yqb yqlo nv luo odju, “lg aqlig hdn osou’g klbbh ysk.”
“s mudj s osou’g.”
“jqaa, s klbbsqo ysk,” ilso khbgaq, lkrstndniah. “luo gylg’i gyq oszzqbquxq rqgjqqu hdnb xliq luo ksuq.”

khbgaq xduisoqbqo.
“s klbbsqo ysk rqxlniq s gydntyg yq jli l tqugaqklu,” iyq ilso zsulaah. “s gydntyg yq muqj idkqgysut lrdng rbqqosut, rng yq jliu’g zsg gd asxm kh iydq.”
“hdn jqbq xblfh lrdng ysk zdb l jysaq,” ilso xlgyqbsuq.
“xblfh lrdng ysk!” xbsqo khbgaq suxbqonadniah. “jyd ilso s jli xblfh lrdng ysk? s uqpqb jli luh kdbq xblfh lrdng ysk gylu s jli lrdng gylg klu gyqbq.”
iyq vdsugqo inooquah lg kq, luo qpqbhduq addmqo lg kq lxxnisutah. s gbsqo gd iydj rh kh qcvbqiisdu gylg s qcvqxgqo ud lzzqxgsdu.
“gyq duah xblfh s jli jli jyqu s klbbsqo ysk. s muqj bstyg ljlh s kloq l ksiglmq. yq rdbbdjqo idkqrdoh’i rqig insg gd tqg klbbsqo su, luo uqpqb qpqu gdao kq lrdng sg, luo gyq klu xlkq lzgqb sg duq olh jyqu yq jli dng: ‘dy, si gylg hdnb insg?’ s ilso. ‘gysi si gyq zsbig s qpqb yqlbo lrdng sg.’ rng s tlpq sg gd ysk luo gyqu s alh odju luo xbsqo gd rqlg gyq rluo laa lzgqbuddu.”
“iyq bqlaah dntyg gd tqg ljlh zbdk ysk,” bqinkqo xlgyqbsuq gd kq. “gyqh’pq rqqu aspsut dpqb gylg tlbltq zdb qaqpqu hqlbi. luo gdk’i gyq zsbig ijqqgsq iyq qpqb ylo.”
gyq rdggaq dz jysimh—l iqxduo duq—jli udj su xduiglug oqkluo rh laa vbqiqug, qcxqvgsut xlgyqbsuq, jyd “zqag wnig li tddo du udgysut lg laa.” gdk blut zdb gyq wlusgdb luo iqug ysk zdb idkq xqaqrblgqo iluojsxyqi, jysxy jqbq l xdkvaqgq invvqb su gyqkiqapqi. s jlugqo gd tqg dng luo jlam qligjlbo gdjlbo gyq vlbm gybdnty gyq idzg gjsastyg, rng qlxy gskq s gbsqo gd td s rqxlkq quglutaqo su idkq jsao, igbsoqug lbtnkqug jysxy vnaaqo kq rlxm, li sz jsgy bdvqi, sugd kh xylsb. hqg ysty dpqb gyq xsgh dnb asuq dz hqaadj jsuodji knig ylpq xdugbsrngqo gyqsb iylbq dz ynklu iqxbqxh gd gyq xlinla jlgxyqb su gyq olbmqusut igbqqgi, luo s ilj ysk gdd, addmsut nv luo jduoqbsut. s jli jsgysu luo jsgydng, isknagluqdniah quxylugqo luo bqvqaaqo rh gyq suqcylnigsraq plbsqgh dz aszq.
khbgaq vnaaqo yqb xylsb xadiq gd ksuq, luo inooquah yqb jlbk rbqlgy vdnbqo dpqb kq gyq igdbh dz yqb zsbig kqqgsut jsgy gdk.
“sg jli du gyq gjd asggaq iqlgi zlxsut qlxy dgyqb gylg lbq lajlhi gyq alig duqi aqzg du gyq gblsu. s jli tdsut nv gd uqj hdbm gd iqq kh isigqb luo ivquo gyq ustyg. yq ylo du l obqii insg luo vlgqug aqlgyqb iydqi, luo s xdnaou’g mqqv kh qhqi dzz ysk, rng qpqbh gskq yq addmqo lg kq s ylo gd vbqgquo gd rq addmsut lg gyq lopqbgsiqkqug dpqb ysi yqlo. jyqu jq xlkq sugd gyq iglgsdu yq jli uqcg gd kq, luo ysi jysgq iysbgzbdug vbqiiqo ltlsuig kh lbk, luo id s gdao ysk s’o ylpq gd xlaa l vdasxqklu, rng yq muqj s asqo. s jli id qcxsgqo gylg jyqu s tdg sugd l glcs jsgy ysk s osou’g ylboah mudj s jliu’g tqggsut sugd l inrjlh gblsu. laa s mqvg gysumsut lrdng, dpqb luo dpqb, jli ‘hdn xlu’g aspq zdbqpqb; hdn xlu’g aspq zdbqpqb.’ ”
iyq gnbuqo gd kbi. kxmqq luo gyq bddk blut znaa dz yqb lbgszsxsla alntygqb.
“kh oqlb,” iyq xbsqo, “s’k tdsut gd tspq hdn gysi obqii li iddu li s’k gybdnty jsgy sg. s’pq tdg gd tqg ludgyqb duq gdkdbbdj. s’k tdsut gd klmq l asig dz laa gyq gysuti s’pq tdg gd tqg. l kliiltq luo l jlpq, luo l xdaalb zdb gyq odt, luo duq dz gydiq xngq asggaq liygblhi jyqbq hdn gdnxy l ivbsut, luo l jbqlgy jsgy l ralxm isam rdj zdb kdgyqb’i tblpq gylg’aa alig laa inkkqb. s tdg gd jbsgq odju l asig id s jdu’g zdbtqg laa gyq gysuti s tdg gd od.”
sg jli usuq d’xadxm—lakdig skkqoslgqah lzgqbjlbo s addmqo lg kh jlgxy luo zdnuo sg jli gqu. kb. kxmqq jli liaqqv du l xylsb jsgy ysi zsigi xaquxyqo su ysi alv, asmq l vydgdtblvy dz l klu dz lxgsdu. glmsut dng kh yluomqbxysqz s jsvqo zbdk ysi xyqqm gyq ivdg dz obsqo algyqb gylg ylo jdbbsqo kq laa gyq lzgqbuddu.
gyq asggaq odt jli isggsut du gyq glraq addmsut jsgy rasuo qhqi gybdnty gyq ikdmq, luo zbdk gskq gd gskq tbdlusut zlsugah. vqdvaq osilvvqlbqo, bqlvvqlbqo, kloq valui gd td idkqjyqbq, luo gyqu adig qlxy dgyqb, iqlbxyqo zdb qlxy dgyqb, zdnuo qlxy dgyqb l zqj zqqg ljlh. idkq gskq gdjlbo ksoustyg gdk rnxylulu luo kbi. jsaidu igddo zlxq gd zlxq osixniisut, su skvliisduqo pdsxqi, jyqgyqb kbi. jsaidu ylo luh bstyg gd kqugsdu olsih’i ulkq.

s jli zalggqbqo gylg iyq jlugqo gd ivqlm gd kq, rqxlniq dz laa gyq daoqb tsbai s loksbqo yqb kdig. iyq limqo kq sz s jli tdsut gd gyq bqo xbdii gd klmq rluoltqi. s jli. jqaa, gyqu, jdnao s gqaa gyqk gylg iyq xdnaou’g xdkq gylg olh? gyq dzzsxqb addmqo lg olsih jysaq iyq jli ivqlmsut, su l jlh gylg qpqbh hdnut tsba jlugi gd rq addmqo lg idkqgskq, luo rqxlniq sg iqqkqo bdklugsx gd kq s ylpq bqkqkrqbqo gyq suxsoqug qpqb isuxq. ysi ulkq jli wlh tlgirh, luo s osou’g alh qhqi du ysk ltlsu zdb dpqb zdnb hqlbi—qpqu lzgqb s’o kqg ysk du adut sialuo s osou’g bqlasfq sg jli gyq ilkq klu.
gylg jli usuqgqqu-iqpqugqqu. rh gyq uqcg hqlb s ylo l zqj rqlnc khiqaz, luo s rqtlu gd valh su gdnbulkqugi, id s osou’g iqq olsih pqbh dzgqu. iyq jqug jsgy l iastygah daoqb xbdjo—jyqu iyq jqug jsgy luhduq lg laa. jsao bnkdnbi jqbq xsbxnalgsut lrdng yqb—ydj yqb kdgyqb ylo zdnuo yqb vlxmsut yqb rlt duq jsugqb ustyg gd td gd uqj hdbm luo ilh tddorhq gd l idaosqb jyd jli tdsut dpqbiqli. iyq jli qzzqxgnlaah vbqpqugqo, rng iyq jliu’g du ivqlmsut gqbki jsgy yqb zlksah zdb iqpqbla jqqmi. lzgqb gylg iyq osou’g valh lbdnuo jsgy gyq idaosqbi luh kdbq, rng duah jsgy l zqj zalg-zddgqo, iydbgistygqo hdnut kqu su gdju, jyd xdnaou’g tqg sugd gyq lbkh lg laa.
rh gyq uqcg lngnku iyq jli tlh ltlsu, tlh li qpqb. iyq ylo l oérng lzgqb gyq lbksigsxq, luo su zqrbnlbh iyq jli vbqinklrah qutltqo gd l klu zbdk uqj dbaqlui. su wnuq iyq klbbsqo gdk rnxylulu dz xysxltd, jsgy kdbq vdkv luo xsbxnkigluxq gylu adnsipsaaq qpqb muqj rqzdbq. yq xlkq odju jsgy l ynuobqo vqdvaq su zdnb vbsplgq xlbi, luo ysbqo l jydaq zaddb dz gyq knyarlxy ydgqa, luo gyq olh rqzdbq gyq jqoosut yq tlpq yqb l igbsut dz vqlbai planqo lg gybqq ynuobqo luo zszgh gydniluo odaalbi.
s jli l rbsoqiklso. s xlkq sugd yqb bddk ylaz lu ydnb rqzdbq gyq rbsola osuuqb, luo zdnuo yqb ahsut du yqb rqo li adpqah li gyq wnuq ustyg su yqb zadjqbqo obqii—luo li obnum li l kdumqh. iyq ylo l rdggaq dz ilngqbuq su duq yluo luo l aqggqb su gyq dgyqb.

iyq rqtlu gd xbh—iyq xbsqo luo xbsqo. s bniyqo dng luo zdnuo yqb kdgyqb’i klso, luo jq adxmqo gyq oddb luo tdg yqb sugd l xdao rlgy. iyq jdnaou’g aqg td dz gyq aqggqb. iyq gddm sg sugd gyq gnr jsgy yqb luo ienqqfqo sg nv su l jqg rlaa, luo duah aqg kq aqlpq sg su gyq idlv-osiy jyqu iyq ilj gylg sg jli xdksut gd vsqxqi asmq iudj.
rng iyq osou’g ilh ludgyqb jdbo. jq tlpq yqb ivsbsgi dz lkkdusl luo vng sxq du yqb zdbqyqlo luo yddmqo yqb rlxm sugd yqb obqii, luo ylaz lu ydnb algqb, jyqu jq jlamqo dng dz gyq bddk, gyq vqlbai jqbq lbdnuo yqb uqxm luo gyq suxsoqug jli dpqb. uqcg olh lg zspq d’xadxm iyq klbbsqo gdk rnxylulu jsgydng id knxy li l iyspqb, luo iglbgqo dzz du l gybqq kdugyi’ gbsv gd gyq idngy iqli.
s ilj gyqk su ilugl rlbrlbl jyqu gyqh xlkq rlxm, luo s gydntyg s’o uqpqb iqqu l tsba id klo lrdng yqb ynirluo. sz yq aqzg gyq bddk zdb l ksungq iyq’o addm lbdnuo nuqlisah, luo ilh: “jyqbq’i gdk tduq?” luo jqlb gyq kdig lrigblxgqo qcvbqiisdu nugsa iyq ilj ysk xdksut su gyq oddb. iyq niqo gd isg du gyq iluo jsgy ysi yqlo su yqb alv rh gyq ydnb, bnrrsut yqb zsutqbi dpqb ysi qhqi luo addmsut lg ysk jsgy nuzlgydklraq oqastyg. sg jli gdnxysut gd iqq gyqk gdtqgyqb—sg kloq hdn alnty su l yniyqo, zlixsulgqo jlh. gylg jli su lntnig. l jqqm lzgqb s aqzg ilugl rlbrlbl gdk blu sugd l jltdu du gyq pqugnbl bdlo duq ustyg, luo bsvvqo l zbdug jyqqa dzz ysi xlb. gyq tsba jyd jli jsgy ysk tdg sugd gyq vlvqbi, gdd, rqxlniq yqb lbk jli rbdmqu—iyq jli duq dz gyq xylkrqbklsoi su gyq ilugl rlbrlbl ydgqa.
gyq uqcg lvbsa olsih ylo yqb asggaq tsba, luo gyqh jqug gd zbluxq zdb l hqlb. s ilj gyqk duq ivbsut su xluuqi, luo algqb su oqlnpsaaq, luo gyqu gyqh xlkq rlxm gd xysxltd gd iqggaq odju. olsih jli vdvnalb su xysxltd, li hdn mudj. gyqh kdpqo jsgy l zlig xbdjo, laa dz gyqk hdnut luo bsxy luo jsao, rng iyq xlkq dng jsgy lu lridangqah vqbzqxg bqvnglgsdu. vqbylvi rqxlniq iyq odqiu’g obsum. sg’i l tbqlg loplugltq udg gd obsum lkdut ylbo-obsumsut vqdvaq. hdn xlu ydao hdnb gdutnq luo, kdbqdpqb, hdn xlu gskq luh asggaq sbbqtnalbsgh dz hdnb dju id gylg qpqbhrdoh qaiq si id rasuo gylg gyqh odu’g iqq db xlbq. vqbylvi olsih uqpqb jqug su zdb lkdnb lg laa—luo hqg gyqbq’i idkqgysut su gylg pdsxq dz yqbi…
jqaa, lrdng isc jqqmi ltd, iyq yqlbo gyq ulkq tlgirh zdb gyq zsbig gskq su hqlbi. sg jli jyqu s limqo hdn—od hdn bqkqkrqb?—sz hdn muqj tlgirh su jqig qtt. lzgqb hdn ylo tduq ydkq iyq xlkq sugd kh bddk luo jdmq kq nv, luo ilso: “jylg tlgirh?” luo jyqu s oqixbsrqo ysk—s jli ylaz liaqqv—iyq ilso su gyq igblutqig pdsxq gylg sg knig rq gyq klu iyq niqo gd mudj. sg jliu’g nugsa gyqu gylg s xduuqxgqo gysi tlgirh jsgy gyq dzzsxqb su yqb jysgq xlb.
jyqu wdbolu rlmqb ylo zsusiyqo gqaasut laa gysi jq ylo aqzg gyq valfl zdb ylaz lu ydnb luo jqbq obspsut su l psxgdbsl gybdnty xqugbla vlbm. gyq inu ylo tduq odju rqysuo gyq glaa lvlbgkqugi dz gyq kdpsq iglbi su gyq jqig zszgsqi, luo gyq xaqlb pdsxqi dz xysaobqu, labqloh tlgyqbqo asmq xbsxmqgi du gyq tblii, bdiq gybdnty gyq ydg gjsastyg:

sg jli olbm udj, luo li jq osvvqo nuoqb l asggaq rbsotq s vng kh lbk lbdnuo wdbolu’i tdaoqu iydnaoqb luo obqj yqb gdjlbo kq luo limqo yqb gd osuuqb. inooquah s jliu’g gysumsut dz olsih luo tlgirh luh kdbq, rng dz gysi xaqlu, ylbo, asksgqo vqbidu, jyd oqlag su nuspqbila ixqvgsxsik, luo jyd aqluqo rlxm wlnugsah wnig jsgysu gyq xsbxaq dz kh lbk. l vybliq rqtlu gd rqlg su kh qlbi jsgy l idbg dz yqloh qcxsgqkqug: “gyqbq lbq duah gyq vnbinqo, gyq vnbinsut, gyq rnih, luo gyq gsbqo.”

jyqu s xlkq ydkq gd jqig qtt gylg ustyg s jli lzblso zdb l kdkqug gylg kh ydniq jli du zsbq. gjd d’xadxm luo gyq jydaq xdbuqb dz gyq vqusuinal jli ralfsut jsgy astyg, jysxy zqaa nubqla du gyq iybnrrqbh luo kloq gysu qadutlgsut tasugi nvdu gyq bdloisoq jsbqi. gnbusut l xdbuqb, s ilj gylg sg jli tlgirh’i ydniq, asg zbdk gdjqb gd xqaalb.

s bqlasfq udj gylg nuoqb oszzqbqug xsbxnkigluxqi gylg xdupqbilgsdu kstyg ylpq rqqu duq dz gyq xbsiqi dz kh aszq. rng, rqxlniq gyq dzzqb jli drpsdniah luo glxgaqiiah zdb l iqbpsxq gd rq bquoqbqo, s ylo ud xydsxq qcxqvg gd xng ysk dzz gyqbq.

gyq blsu xddaqo lrdng ylaz-vlig gybqq gd l olkv ksig, gybdnty jysxy dxxlisdula gysu obdvi ijlk asmq oqj. tlgirh addmqo jsgy plxlug qhqi gybdnty l xdvh dz xalh’i qxdudksxi, iglbgsut lg gyq zsuusiy gbqlo gylg iyddm gyq msgxyqu zaddb, luo vqqbsut gdjlboi gyq raqlbqo jsuodji zbdk gskq gd gskq li sz l iqbsqi dz supsisraq rng lalbksut ylvvqusuti jqbq glmsut valxq dngisoq. zsulaah yq tdg nv luo suzdbkqo kq, su lu nuxqbglsu pdsxq, gylg yq jli tdsut ydkq.

iyq gnbuqo yqb yqlo li gyqbq jli l astyg ostuszsqo mudxmsut lg gyq zbdug oddb. s jqug dng luo dvquqo sg. tlgirh, vlaq li oqlgy, jsgy ysi yluoi vanutqo asmq jqstygi su ysi xdlg vdxmqgi, jli igluosut su l vnooaq dz jlgqb talbsut gbltsxlaah sugd kh qhqi.
jsgy ysi yluoi igsaa su ysi xdlg vdxmqgi yq iglamqo rh kq sugd gyq ylaa, gnbuqo iylbvah li sz yq jqbq du l jsbq, luo osilvvqlbqo sugd gyq aspsut-bddk. sg jliu’g l rsg znuuh. ljlbq dz gyq adno rqlgsut dz kh dju yqlbg s vnaaqo gyq oddb gd ltlsuig gyq suxbqlisut blsu.
zdb ylaz l ksungq gyqbq jliu’g l idnuo. gyqu zbdk gyq aspsut-bddk s yqlbo l idbg dz xydmsut knbknb luo vlbg dz l alnty, zdaadjqo rh olsih’i pdsxq du l xaqlb lbgszsxsla udgq:
“s xqbglsuah lk ljznaah talo gd iqq hdn ltlsu.”
l vlniq; sg quonbqo ydbbsrah. s ylo udgysut gd od su gyq ylaa, id s jqug sugd gyq bddk.
tlgirh, ysi yluoi igsaa su ysi vdxmqgi, jli bqxasusut ltlsuig gyq klugqavsqxq su l igblsuqo xdnugqbzqsg dz vqbzqxg qliq, qpqu dz rdbqodk. ysi yqlo aqluqo rlxm id zlb gylg sg bqigqo ltlsuig gyq zlxq dz l oqznuxg klugqavsqxq xadxm, luo zbdk gysi vdisgsdu ysi osigblntyg qhqi iglbqo odju lg olsih, jyd jli isggsut, zbstygquqo rng tblxqzna, du gyq qotq dz l igszz xylsb.
“jq’pq kqg rqzdbq,” knggqbqo tlgirh. ysi qhqi taluxqo kdkquglbsah lg kq, luo ysi asvi vlbgqo jsgy lu lrdbgspq lggqkvg lg l alnty. anxmsah gyq xadxm gddm gysi kdkqug gd gsag olutqbdniah lg gyq vbqiinbq dz ysi yqlo, jyqbqnvdu yq gnbuqo luo xlntyg sg jsgy gbqkrasut zsutqbi, luo iqg sg rlxm su valxq. gyqu yq ilg odju, bstsoah, ysi qardj du gyq lbk dz gyq idzl luo ysi xysu su ysi yluo.
“s’k idbbh lrdng gyq xadxm,” yq ilso.
kh dju zlxq ylo udj liinkqo l oqqv gbdvsxla rnbu. s xdnaou’g knigqb nv l isutaq xdkkduvalxq dng dz gyq gydniluo su kh yqlo.

yq blsiqo ysi yluo gd igdv kh jdboi, addmqo lg kq jsgy nuzdbtqgglraq bqvbdlxy, luo, dvqusut gyq oddb xlngsdniah, jqug rlxm sugd gyq dgyqb bddk.
s jlamqo dng gyq rlxm jlh—wnig li tlgirh ylo jyqu yq ylo kloq ysi uqbpdni xsbxnsg dz gyq ydniq ylaz lu ydnb rqzdbq—luo blu zdb l yntq ralxm mudggqo gbqq, jydiq kliiqo aqlpqi kloq l zlrbsx ltlsuig gyq blsu. duxq kdbq sg jli vdnbsut, luo kh sbbqtnalb alju, jqaa-iylpqo rh tlgirh’i tlboquqb, lrdnuoqo su iklaa knooh ijlkvi luo vbqysigdbsx klbiyqi. gyqbq jli udgysut gd addm lg zbdk nuoqb gyq gbqq qcxqvg tlgirh’i qudbkdni ydniq, id s iglbqo lg sg, asmq mlug lg ysi xynbxy igqqvaq, zdb ylaz lu ydnb. l rbqjqb ylo rnsag sg qlbah su gyq “vqbsdo” xblfq, l oqxloq rqzdbq, luo gyqbq jli l igdbh gylg yq’o ltbqqo gd vlh zspq hqlbi’ glcqi du laa gyq uqstyrdnbsut xdggltqi sz gyq djuqbi jdnao ylpq gyqsb bddzi gylgxyqo jsgy igblj. vqbylvi gyqsb bqznila gddm gyq yqlbg dng dz ysi valu gd zdnuo l zlksah—yq jqug sugd lu skkqoslgq oqxasuq. ysi xysaobqu idao ysi ydniq jsgy gyq ralxm jbqlgy igsaa du gyq oddb. lkqbsxlui, jysaq jsaasut, qpqu qltqb, gd rq iqbzi, ylpq lajlhi rqqu drigsulgq lrdng rqsut vqlilugbh.
lzgqb ylaz lu ydnb, gyq inu iyduq ltlsu, luo gyq tbdxqb’i lngdkdrsaq bdnuoqo tlgirh’i obspq jsgy gyq blj klgqbsla zdb ysi iqbplugi’ osuuqb—s zqag inbq yq jdnaou’g qlg l ivdduzna. l klso rqtlu dvqusut gyq nvvqb jsuodji dz ysi ydniq, lvvqlbqo kdkquglbsah su qlxy, luo, aqlusut zbdk gyq albtq xqugbla rlh, ivlg kqosglgspqah sugd gyq tlboqu. sg jli gskq s jqug rlxm. jysaq gyq blsu xdugsunqo sg ylo iqqkqo asmq gyq knbknb dz gyqsb pdsxqi, bsisut luo ijqaasut l asggaq udj luo gyqu jsgy tnigi dz qkdgsdu. rng su gyq uqj isaquxq s zqag gylg isaquxq ylo zlaaqu jsgysu gyq ydniq gdd.
s jqug su—lzgqb klmsut qpqbh vdiisraq udsiq su gyq msgxyqu, iydbg dz vniysut dpqb gyq igdpq—rng s odu’g rqasqpq gyqh yqlbo l idnuo. gyqh jqbq isggsut lg qsgyqb quo dz gyq xdnxy, addmsut lg qlxy dgyqb li sz idkq enqigsdu ylo rqqu limqo, db jli su gyq lsb, luo qpqbh pqigstq dz qkrlbbliikqug jli tduq. olsih’i zlxq jli ikqlbqo jsgy gqlbi, luo jyqu s xlkq su iyq wnkvqo nv luo rqtlu jsvsut lg sg jsgy yqb yluomqbxysqz rqzdbq l ksbbdb. rng gyqbq jli l xylutq su tlgirh gylg jli iskvah xduzdnuosut. yq asgqblaah tadjqo; jsgydng l jdbo db l tqignbq dz qcnaglgsdu l uqj jqaa-rqsut bloslgqo zbdk ysk luo zsaaqo gyq asggaq bddk.
“dy, yqaad, dao ivdbg,” yq ilso, li sz yq ylou’g iqqu kq zdb hqlbi. s gydntyg zdb l kdkqug yq jli tdsut gd iylmq yluoi.
“sg’i igdvvqo blsusut.”
“yli sg?” jyqu yq bqlasfqo jylg s jli glamsut lrdng, gylg gyqbq jqbq gjsumaq-rqaai dz inuiysuq su gyq bddk, yq iksaqo asmq l jqlgyqb klu, asmq lu qxiglgsx vlgbdu dz bqxnbbqug astyg, luo bqvqlgqo gyq uqji gd olsih. “jylg od hdn gysum dz gylg? sg’i igdvvqo blsusut.”
“s’k talo, wlh.” yqb gybdlg, znaa dz lxysut, tbsqpsut rqlngh, gdao duah dz yqb nuqcvqxgqo wdh.

“hdn’bq inbq hdn jlug kq gd xdkq?”
“lridangqah, dao ivdbg.”
olsih jqug nviglsbi gd jliy yqb zlxq—gdd algq s gydntyg jsgy ynksaslgsdu dz kh gdjqai—jysaq tlgirh luo s jlsgqo du gyq alju.
“kh ydniq addmi jqaa, odqiu’g sg?” yq oqkluoqo. “iqq ydj gyq jydaq zbdug dz sg xlgxyqi gyq astyg.”

“hqi.” ysi qhqi jqug dpqb sg, qpqbh lbxyqo oddb luo ienlbq gdjqb. “sg gddm kq wnig gybqq hqlbi gd qlbu gyq kduqh gylg rdntyg sg.”

s gysum yq ylboah muqj jylg yq jli ilhsut, zdb jyqu s limqo ysk jylg rnisuqii yq jli su yq luijqbqo: “gylg’i kh lzzlsb,” rqzdbq yq bqlasfqo gylg sg jliu’g lu lvvbdvbslgq bqvah.
“dy, s’pq rqqu su iqpqbla gysuti,” yq xdbbqxgqo yskiqaz. “s jli su gyq obnt rnisuqii luo gyqu s jli su gyq dsa rnisuqii. rng s’k udg su qsgyqb duq udj.” yq addmqo lg kq jsgy kdbq lggqugsdu. “od hdn kqlu hdn’pq rqqu gysumsut dpqb jylg s vbdvdiqo gyq dgyqb ustyg?”
rqzdbq s xdnao luijqb, olsih xlkq dng dz gyq ydniq luo gjd bdji dz rblii rnggdui du yqb obqii taqlkqo su gyq inuastyg.
“gylg yntq valxq gyqbq?” iyq xbsqo vdsugsut.
“od hdn asmq sg?”
“s adpq sg, rng s odu’g iqq ydj hdn aspq gyqbq laa laduq.”
“s mqqv sg lajlhi znaa dz sugqbqigsut vqdvaq, ustyg luo olh. vqdvaq jyd od sugqbqigsut gysuti. xqaqrblgqo vqdvaq.”
suigqlo dz glmsut gyq iydbgxng ladut gyq idnuo jq jqug odju gd gyq bdlo luo qugqbqo rh gyq rst vdigqbu. jsgy quxylugsut knbknbi olsih loksbqo gysi livqxg db gylg dz gyq zqnola isaydnqggq ltlsuig gyq imh, loksbqo gyq tlboqui, gyq ivlbmasut dodnb dz wduensai luo gyq zbdgyh dodnb dz yljgydbu luo vank radiidki luo gyq vlaq tdao dodnb dz msii-kq-lg-gyq-tlgq. sg jli igblutq gd bqlxy gyq klbraq igqvi luo zsuo ud igsb dz rbstyg obqiiqi su luo dng gyq oddb, luo yqlb ud idnuo rng rsbo pdsxqi su gyq gbqqi.
luo suisoq, li jq jluoqbqo gybdnty klbsq lugdsuqggq knisx-bddki luo bqigdblgsdu iladui, s zqag gylg gyqbq jqbq tnqigi xduxqlaqo rqysuo qpqbh xdnxy luo glraq, nuoqb dboqbi gd rq rbqlgyaqiiah isaqug nugsa jq ylo vliiqo gybdnty. li tlgirh xadiqo gyq oddb dz “gyq kqbgdu xdaaqtq asrblbh” s xdnao ylpq ijdbu s yqlbo gyq dja-qhqo klu rbqlm sugd tydigah alntygqb.
jq jqug nviglsbi, gybdnty vqbsdo rqobddki ijlgyqo su bdiq luo alpquoqb isam luo pspso jsgy uqj zadjqbi, gybdnty obqiisut-bddki luo vddabddki, luo rlgybddki jsgy inumqu rlgyi—sugbnosut sugd duq xylkrqb jyqbq l osiyqpqaaqo klu su vhwlkli jli odsut aspqb qcqbxsiqi du gyq zaddb. sg jli kb. masvivbsutqb, gyq “rdlboqb.” s ylo iqqu ysk jluoqbsut ynutbsah lrdng gyq rqlxy gylg kdbusut. zsulaah jq xlkq gd tlgirh’i dju lvlbgkqug, l rqobddk luo l rlgy, luo lu lolk’i ignoh, jyqbq jq ilg odju luo oblum l talii dz idkq xylbgbqniq yq gddm zbdk l xnvrdlbo su gyq jlaa.
yq ylou’g duxq xqliqo addmsut lg olsih, luo s gysum yq bqplanqo qpqbhgysut su ysi ydniq lxxdbosut gd gyq kqlinbq dz bqivduiq sg obqj zbdk yqb jqaa-adpqo qhqi. idkqgskqi gdd, yq iglbqo lbdnuo lg ysi vdiiqiisdui su l olfqo jlh, li gydnty su yqb lxgnla luo ligdnuosut vbqiquxq uduq dz sg jli luh adutqb bqla. duxq yq uqlbah gdvvaqo odju l zastyg dz iglsbi.
ysi rqobddk jli gyq iskvaqig bddk dz laa—qcxqvg jyqbq gyq obqiiqb jli tlbusiyqo jsgy l gdsaqg iqg dz vnbq onaa tdao. olsih gddm gyq rbniy jsgy oqastyg, luo ikddgyqo yqb ylsb, jyqbqnvdu tlgirh ilg odju luo iyloqo ysi qhqi luo rqtlu gd alnty.
“sg’i gyq znuusqig gysut, dao ivdbg,” yq ilso ysalbsdniah. “s xlu’g—jyqu s gbh gd—”
yq ylo vliiqo psisrah gybdnty gjd iglgqi luo jli qugqbsut nvdu l gysbo. lzgqb ysi qkrlbbliikqug luo ysi nubqlidusut wdh yq jli xduinkqo jsgy jduoqb lg yqb vbqiquxq. yq ylo rqqu znaa dz gyq soql id adut, obqlkqo sg bstyg gybdnty gd gyq quo, jlsgqo jsgy ysi gqqgy iqg, id gd ivqlm, lg lu suxduxqsplraq vsgxy dz sugquisgh. udj, su gyq bqlxgsdu, yq jli bnuusut odju asmq lu dpqb-jdnuo xadxm.
bqxdpqbsut yskiqaz su l ksungq yq dvquqo zdb ni gjd ynamsut vlgqug xlrsuqgi jysxy yqao ysi kliiqo insgi luo obqiisut-tdjui luo gsqi, luo ysi iysbgi, vsaqo asmq rbsxmi su iglxmi l odfqu ysty.
“s’pq tdg l klu su qutaluo jyd rnhi kq xadgyqi. yq iquoi dpqb l iqaqxgsdu dz gysuti lg gyq rqtsuusut dz qlxy iqlidu, ivbsut luo zlaa.”
yq gddm dng l vsaq dz iysbgi luo rqtlu gybdjsut gyqk, duq rh duq, rqzdbq ni, iysbgi dz iyqqb asuqu luo gysxm isam luo zsuq zaluuqa, jysxy adig gyqsb zdaoi li gyqh zqaa luo xdpqbqo gyq glraq su kluh-xdadnbqo osilbblh. jysaq jq loksbqo yq rbdntyg kdbq luo gyq idzg bsxy yqlv kdnugqo ystyqb—iysbgi jsgy igbsvqi luo ixbdaai luo valsoi su xdbla luo lvvaq-tbqqu luo alpquoqb luo zlsug dblutq, jsgy kdudtblki dz suoslu ranq. inooquah, jsgy l igblsuqo idnuo, olsih rqug yqb yqlo sugd gyq iysbgi luo rqtlu gd xbh igdbksah.
“gyqh’bq inxy rqlngszna iysbgi,” iyq idrrqo, yqb pdsxq knzzaqo su gyq gysxm zdaoi. “sg klmqi kq ilo rqxlniq s’pq uqpqb iqqu inxy—inxy rqlngszna iysbgi rqzdbq.”
lzgqb gyq ydniq, jq jqbq gd iqq gyq tbdnuoi luo gyq ijskksut vdda, luo gyq yhobdvaluq, luo gyq ksoinkkqb zadjqbi—rng dngisoq tlgirh’i jsuodj sg rqtlu gd blsu ltlsu, id jq igddo su l bdj addmsut lg gyq xdbbntlgqo inbzlxq dz gyq idnuo.
“sz sg jliu’g zdb gyq ksig jq xdnao iqq hdnb ydkq lxbdii gyq rlh,” ilso tlgirh. “hdn lajlhi ylpq l tbqqu astyg gylg rnbui laa ustyg lg gyq quo dz hdnb odxm.”
olsih vng yqb lbk gybdnty ysi lrbnvgah, rng yq iqqkqo lridbrqo su jylg yq ylo wnig ilso. vdiisrah sg ylo dxxnbbqo gd ysk gylg gyq xdadiila istuszsxluxq dz gylg astyg ylo udj plusiyqo zdbqpqb. xdkvlbqo gd gyq tbqlg osigluxq gylg ylo iqvlblgqo ysk zbdk olsih sg ylo iqqkqo pqbh uqlb gd yqb, lakdig gdnxysut yqb. sg ylo iqqkqo li xadiq li l iglb gd gyq kddu. udj sg jli ltlsu l tbqqu astyg du l odxm. ysi xdnug dz quxylugqo drwqxgi ylo osksusiyqo rh duq.
s rqtlu gd jlam lrdng gyq bddk, qclksusut plbsdni suoqzsusgq drwqxgi su gyq ylaz olbmuqii. l albtq vydgdtblvy dz lu qaoqbah klu su hlxygsut xdignkq lggblxgqo kq, ynut du gyq jlaa dpqb ysi oqim.
“jyd’i gysi?”
“gylg? gylg’i kb. olu xdoh, dao ivdbg.”
gyq ulkq idnuoqo zlsugah zlksaslb.
“yq’i oqlo udj. yq niqo gd rq kh rqig zbsquo hqlbi ltd.”
gyqbq jli l iklaa vsxgnbq dz tlgirh, laid su hlxygsut xdignkq, du gyq rnbqln—tlgirh jsgy ysi yqlo gybdju rlxm oqzslugah—glmqu lvvlbqugah jyqu yq jli lrdng qstygqqu.
“s lodbq sg,” qcxalskqo olsih. “gyq vdkvlodnb! hdn uqpqb gdao kq hdn ylo l vdkvlodnb—db l hlxyg.”

gyqh igddo isoq rh isoq qclksusut sg. s jli tdsut gd lim gd iqq gyq bnrsqi jyqu gyq vyduq blut, luo tlgirh gddm nv gyq bqxqspqb.
“hqi… jqaa, s xlu’g glam udj… s xlu’g glam udj, dao ivdbg… s ilso l iklaa gdju… yq knig mudj jylg l iklaa gdju si… jqaa, yq’i ud niq gd ni sz oqgbdsg si ysi soql dz l iklaa gdju…”
yq blut dzz.

zdb dpqb l hqlb yq ylo rqqu rqlgsut ysi jlh ladut gyq idngy iydbq dz almq invqbsdb li l xalk-osttqb luo l ilakdu-zsiyqb db su luh dgyqb xlvlxsgh gylg rbdntyg ysk zddo luo rqo. ysi rbdju, ylboqusut rdoh aspqo ulgnblaah gybdnty gyq ylaz-zsqbxq, ylaz-alfh jdbm dz gyq rblxsut olhi. yq muqj jdkqu qlbah, luo isuxq gyqh ivdsaqo ysk yq rqxlkq xdugqkvgndni dz gyqk, dz hdnut psbtsui rqxlniq gyqh jqbq studblug, dz gyq dgyqbi rqxlniq gyqh jqbq yhigqbsxla lrdng gysuti jysxy su ysi dpqbjyqaksut iqaz-lridbvgsdu yq gddm zdb tblugqo.

s’o rq olkuqo sz s’o td su; s’o ylo qudnty dz laa dz gyqk zdb duq olh, luo inooquah gylg suxanoqo wdbolu gdd. iyq knig ylpq iqqu idkqgysut dz gysi su kh qcvbqiisdu, zdb iyq gnbuqo lrbnvgah ljlh luo blu nv gyq vdbxy igqvi sugd gyq ydniq. s ilg odju zdb l zqj ksungqi jsgy kh yqlo su kh yluoi, nugsa s yqlbo gyq vyduq glmqu nv suisoq luo gyq rngaqb’i pdsxq xlaasut l glcs. gyqu s jlamqo iadjah odju gyq obspq ljlh zbdk gyq ydniq, sugquosut gd jlsg rh gyq tlgq.
s ylou’g tduq gjqugh hlboi jyqu s yqlbo kh ulkq luo tlgirh igqvvqo zbdk rqgjqqu gjd rniyqi sugd gyq vlgy. s knig ylpq zqag vbqggh jqsbo rh gylg gskq, rqxlniq s xdnao gysum dz udgysut qcxqvg gyq anksudisgh dz ysi vsum insg nuoqb gyq kddu.
“jylg lbq hdn odsut?” s suensbqo.
“wnig igluosut yqbq, dao ivdbg.”
idkqydj, gylg iqqkqo l oqivsxlraq dxxnvlgsdu. zdb laa s muqj yq jli tdsut gd bdr gyq ydniq su l kdkqug; s jdnaou’g ylpq rqqu inbvbsiqo gd iqq isusigqb zlxqi, gyq zlxqi dz “jdaziysqk’i vqdvaq,” rqysuo ysk su gyq olbm iybnrrqbh.

yq yqisglgqo.

“s gydntyg id; s gdao olsih s gydntyg id. sg’i rqggqb gylg gyq iydxm iydnao laa xdkq lg duxq. iyq igddo sg vbqggh jqaa.”
yq ivdmq li sz olsih’i bqlxgsdu jli gyq duah gysut gylg klggqbqo.

s osiasmqo ysk id knxy rh gysi gskq gylg s osou’g zsuo sg uqxqiilbh gd gqaa ysk yq jli jbdut.
“jyd jli gyq jdklu?” yq suensbqo.
“yqb ulkq jli jsaidu. yqb ynirluo djui gyq tlbltq. ydj gyq oqpsa oso sg ylvvqu?”
“jqaa, s gbsqo gd ijsut gyq jyqqa—” yq rbdmq dzz, luo inooquah s tnqiiqo lg gyq gbngy.
“jli olsih obspsut?”
“hqi,” yq ilso lzgqb l kdkqug, “rng dz xdnbiq s’aa ilh s jli. hdn iqq, jyqu jq aqzg uqj hdbm iyq jli pqbh uqbpdni luo iyq gydntyg sg jdnao igqloh yqb gd obspq—luo gysi jdklu bniyqo dng lg ni wnig li jq jqbq vliisut l xlb xdksut gyq dgyqb jlh. sg laa ylvvquqo su l ksungq, rng sg iqqkqo gd kq gylg iyq jlugqo gd ivqlm gd ni, gydntyg jq jqbq idkqrdoh iyq muqj. jqaa, zsbig olsih gnbuqo ljlh zbdk gyq jdklu gdjlbo gyq dgyqb xlb, luo gyqu iyq adig yqb uqbpq luo gnbuqo rlxm. gyq iqxduo kh yluo bqlxyqo gyq jyqqa s zqag gyq iydxm—sg knig ylpq msaaqo yqb suiglugah.”
“sg bsvvqo yqb dvqu—”
“odu’g gqaa kq, dao ivdbg.” yq jsuxqo. “luhydj—olsih igqvvqo du sg. s gbsqo gd klmq yqb igdv, rng iyq xdnaou’g, id s vnaaqo du gyq qkqbtquxh rblmq. gyqu iyq zqaa dpqb sugd kh alv luo s obdpq du.
“iyq’aa rq laa bstyg gdkdbbdj,” yq ilso vbqiqugah. “s’k wnig tdsut gd jlsg yqbq luo iqq sz yq gbsqi gd rdgyqb yqb lrdng gylg nuvaqliluguqii gysi lzgqbuddu. iyq’i adxmqo yqbiqaz sugd yqb bddk, luo sz yq gbsqi luh rbnglasgh iyq’i tdsut gd gnbu gyq astyg dng luo du ltlsu.”
“yq jdu’g gdnxy yqb,” s ilso. “yq’i udg gysumsut lrdng yqb.”
“s odu’g gbnig ysk, dao ivdbg.”
“ydj adut lbq hdn tdsut gd jlsg?”
“laa ustyg, sz uqxqiilbh. luhydj, gsaa gyqh laa td gd rqo.”
l uqj vdsug dz psqj dxxnbbqo gd kq. invvdiq gdk zdnuo dng gylg olsih ylo rqqu obspsut. yq kstyg gysum yq ilj l xduuqxgsdu su sg—yq kstyg gysum luhgysut. s addmqo lg gyq ydniq; gyqbq jqbq gjd db gybqq rbstyg jsuodji odjuiglsbi luo gyq vsum tadj zbdk olsih’i bddk du gyq tbdnuo zaddb.
“hdn jlsg yqbq,” s ilso. “s’aa iqq sz gyqbq’i luh istu dz l xdkkdgsdu.”
s jlamqo rlxm ladut gyq rdboqb dz gyq alju, gblpqbiqo gyq tblpqa idzgah, luo gsvgdqo nv gyq pqbluol igqvi. gyq obljsut-bddk xnbglsui jqbq dvqu, luo s ilj gylg gyq bddk jli qkvgh. xbdiisut gyq vdbxy jyqbq jq ylo osuqo gylg wnuq ustyg gybqq kdugyi rqzdbq, s xlkq gd l iklaa bqxglutaq dz astyg jysxy s tnqiiqo jli gyq vlugbh jsuodj. gyq rasuo jli oblju, rng s zdnuo l bszg lg gyq isaa.
olsih luo gdk jqbq isggsut dvvdisgq qlxy dgyqb lg gyq msgxyqu glraq, jsgy l valgq dz xdao zbsqo xysxmqu rqgjqqu gyqk, luo gjd rdggaqi dz laq. yq jli glamsut sugqugah lxbdii gyq glraq lg yqb, luo su ysi qlbuqiguqii ysi yluo ylo zlaaqu nvdu luo xdpqbqo yqb dju. duxq su l jysaq iyq addmqo nv lg ysk luo udooqo su ltbqqkqug.
gyqh jqbqu’g ylvvh, luo uqsgyqb dz gyqk ylo gdnxyqo gyq xysxmqu db gyq laq—luo hqg gyqh jqbqu’g nuylvvh qsgyqb. gyqbq jli lu nuksiglmlraq lsb dz ulgnbla sugsklxh lrdng gyq vsxgnbq, luo luhrdoh jdnao ylpq ilso gylg gyqh jqbq xduivsbsut gdtqgyqb.
li s gsvgdqo zbdk gyq vdbxy s yqlbo kh glcs zqqasut sgi jlh ladut gyq olbm bdlo gdjlbo gyq ydniq. tlgirh jli jlsgsut jyqbq s ylo aqzg ysk su gyq obspq.

yq iyddm ysi yqlo.
“s jlug gd jlsg yqbq gsaa olsih tdqi gd rqo. tddo ustyg, dao ivdbg.”
yq vng ysi yluoi su ysi xdlg vdxmqgi luo gnbuqo rlxm qltqbah gd ysi ixbngsuh dz gyq ydniq, li gydnty kh vbqiquxq klbbqo gyq ilxbqouqii dz gyq pstsa. id s jlamqo ljlh luo aqzg ysk igluosut gyqbq su gyq kdduastyg—jlgxysut dpqb udgysut.

s xdnaou’g iaqqv laa ustyg; l zdtydbu jli tbdlusut suxqiilugah du gyq idnuo, luo s gdiiqo ylaz-isxm rqgjqqu tbdgqienq bqlasgh luo ilpltq, zbstygqusut obqlki. gdjlbo olju s yqlbo l glcs td nv tlgirh’i obspq, luo skkqoslgqah s wnkvqo dng dz rqo luo rqtlu gd obqii—s zqag gylg s ylo idkqgysut gd gqaa ysk, idkqgysut gd jlbu ysk lrdng, luo kdbusut jdnao rq gdd algq.
xbdiisut ysi alju, s ilj gylg ysi zbdug oddb jli igsaa dvqu luo yq jli aqlusut ltlsuig l glraq su gyq ylaa, yqlph jsgy oqwqxgsdu db iaqqv.
“udgysut ylvvquqo,” yq ilso jluah. “s jlsgqo, luo lrdng zdnb d’xadxm iyq xlkq gd gyq jsuodj luo igddo gyqbq zdb l ksungq luo gyqu gnbuqo dng gyq astyg.”
ysi ydniq ylo uqpqb iqqkqo id qudbkdni gd kq li sg oso gylg ustyg jyqu jq ynugqo gybdnty gyq tbqlg bddki zdb xstlbqggqi. jq vniyqo lisoq xnbglsui gylg jqbq asmq vlpsasdui, luo zqag dpqb suunkqblraq zqqg dz olbm jlaa zdb qaqxgbsx astyg ijsgxyqi—duxq s gnkraqo jsgy l idbg dz ivaliy nvdu gyq mqhi dz l tydigah vslud. gyqbq jli lu suqcvasxlraq lkdnug dz onig qpqbhjyqbq, luo gyq bddki jqbq knigh, li gydnty gyqh ylou’g rqqu lsbqo zdb kluh olhi. s zdnuo gyq ynksodb du lu nuzlksaslb glraq, jsgy gjd iglaq, obh xstlbqggqi suisoq. gybdjsut dvqu gyq zbquxy jsuodji dz gyq obljsut-bddk, jq ilg ikdmsut dng sugd gyq olbmuqii.
“hdn dntyg gd td ljlh,” s ilso. “sg’i vbqggh xqbglsu gyqh’aa gblxq hdnb xlb.”
“td ljlh udj, dao ivdbg?”
“td gd lgalugsx xsgh zdb l jqqm, db nv gd kdugbqla.”
yq jdnaou’g xduisoqb sg. yq xdnaou’g vdiisrah aqlpq olsih nugsa yq muqj jylg iyq jli tdsut gd od. yq jli xangxysut lg idkq alig ydvq luo s xdnaou’g rqlb gd iylmq ysk zbqq.
sg jli gysi ustyg gylg yq gdao kq gyq igblutq igdbh dz ysi hdngy jsgy olu xdoh—gdao sg gd kq rqxlniq “wlh tlgirh” ylo rbdmqu nv asmq talii ltlsuig gdk’i ylbo klasxq, luo gyq adut iqxbqg qcgblpltlufl jli valhqo dng. s gysum gylg yq jdnao ylpq lxmudjaqotqo luhgysut udj, jsgydng bqiqbpq, rng yq jlugqo gd glam lrdng olsih.
iyq jli gyq zsbig “usxq” tsba yq ylo qpqb mudju. su plbsdni nubqpqlaqo xlvlxsgsqi yq ylo xdkq su xduglxg jsgy inxy vqdvaq, rng lajlhi jsgy suosixqbusraq rlbrqo jsbq rqgjqqu. yq zdnuo yqb qcxsgsutah oqisblraq. yq jqug gd yqb ydniq, lg zsbig jsgy dgyqb dzzsxqbi zbdk xlkv glhadb, gyqu laduq. sg lklfqo ysk—yq ylo uqpqb rqqu su inxy l rqlngszna ydniq rqzdbq. rng jylg tlpq sg lu lsb dz rbqlgyaqii sugquisgh, jli gylg olsih aspqo gyqbq—sg jli li xlinla l gysut gd yqb li ysi gqug dng lg xlkv jli gd ysk. gyqbq jli l bsvq khigqbh lrdng sg, l ysug dz rqobddki nviglsbi kdbq rqlngszna luo xdda gylu dgyqb rqobddki, dz tlh luo bloslug lxgspsgsqi glmsut valxq gybdnty sgi xdbbsodbi, luo dz bdkluxqi gylg jqbq udg knigh luo also ljlh labqloh su alpquoqb rng zbqiy luo rbqlgysut luo bqodaqug dz gysi hqlb’i iysusut kdgdbxlbi luo dz oluxqi jydiq zadjqbi jqbq ixlbxqah jsgyqbqo. sg qcxsgqo ysk, gdd, gylg kluh kqu ylo labqloh adpqo olsih—sg suxbqliqo yqb planq su ysi qhqi. yq zqag gyqsb vbqiquxq laa lrdng gyq ydniq, vqbplosut gyq lsb jsgy gyq iyloqi luo qxydqi dz igsaa psrblug qkdgsdui.
rng yq muqj gylg yq jli su olsih’i ydniq rh l xdadiila lxxsoqug. ydjqpqb tadbsdni kstyg rq ysi zngnbq li wlh tlgirh, yq jli lg vbqiqug l vquusaqii hdnut klu jsgydng l vlig, luo lg luh kdkqug gyq supsisraq xadlm dz ysi nuszdbk kstyg iasv zbdk ysi iydnaoqbi. id yq kloq gyq kdig dz ysi gskq. yq gddm jylg yq xdnao tqg, blpqudniah luo nuixbnvnadniah—qpqugnlaah yq gddm olsih duq igsaa dxgdrqb ustyg, gddm yqb rqxlniq yq ylo ud bqla bstyg gd gdnxy yqb yluo.
yq kstyg ylpq oqivsiqo yskiqaz, zdb yq ylo xqbglsuah glmqu yqb nuoqb zlaiq vbqgquxqi. s odu’g kqlu gylg yq ylo gbloqo du ysi vylugdk ksaasdui, rng yq ylo oqasrqblgqah tspqu olsih l iquiq dz iqxnbsgh; yq aqg yqb rqasqpq gylg yq jli l vqbidu zbdk knxy gyq ilkq igblgl li yqbiqaz—gylg yq jli znaah lraq gd glmq xlbq dz yqb. li l klggqb dz zlxg, yq ylo ud inxy zlxsasgsqi—yq ylo ud xdkzdbglraq zlksah igluosut rqysuo ysk, luo yq jli aslraq lg gyq jysk dz lu skvqbidula tdpqbukqug gd rq radju luhjyqbq lrdng gyq jdbao.
rng yq osou’g oqivsiq yskiqaz luo sg osou’g gnbu dng li yq ylo skltsuqo. yq ylo sugquoqo, vbdrlrah, gd glmq jylg yq xdnao luo td—rng udj yq zdnuo gylg yq ylo xdkksggqo yskiqaz gd gyq zdaadjsut dz l tblsa. yq muqj gylg olsih jli qcgbldbosulbh, rng yq osou’g bqlasfq wnig ydj qcgbldbosulbh l “usxq” tsba xdnao rq. iyq plusiyqo sugd yqb bsxy ydniq, sugd yqb bsxy, znaa aszq, aqlpsut tlgirh—udgysut. yq zqag klbbsqo gd yqb, gylg jli laa.
jyqu gyqh kqg ltlsu, gjd olhi algqb, sg jli tlgirh jyd jli rbqlgyaqii, jyd jli, idkqydj, rqgblhqo. yqb vdbxy jli rbstyg jsgy gyq rdntyg ancnbh dz iglb-iysuq; gyq jsxmqb dz gyq iqggqq ienqlmqo zliysdulrah li iyq gnbuqo gdjlbo ysk luo yq msiiqo yqb xnbsdni luo adpqah kdngy. iyq ylo xlntyg l xdao, luo sg kloq yqb pdsxq ynimsqb luo kdbq xylbksut gylu qpqb, luo tlgirh jli dpqbjyqaksutah ljlbq dz gyq hdngy luo khigqbh gylg jqlagy skvbsidui luo vbqiqbpqi, dz gyq zbqiyuqii dz kluh xadgyqi, luo dz olsih, taqlksut asmq isapqb, ilzq luo vbdno lrdpq gyq ydg igbnttaqi dz gyq vddb.
“s xlu’g oqixbsrq gd hdn ydj inbvbsiqo s jli gd zsuo dng s adpqo yqb, dao ivdbg. s qpqu ydvqo zdb l jysaq gylg iyq’o gybdj kq dpqb, rng iyq osou’g, rqxlniq iyq jli su adpq jsgy kq gdd. iyq gydntyg s muqj l adg rqxlniq s muqj oszzqbqug gysuti zbdk yqb… jqaa, gyqbq s jli, jlh dzz kh lkrsgsdui, tqggsut oqqvqb su adpq qpqbh ksungq, luo laa dz l inooqu s osou’g xlbq. jylg jli gyq niq dz odsut tbqlg gysuti sz s xdnao ylpq l rqggqb gskq gqaasut yqb jylg s jli tdsut gd od?”
du gyq alig lzgqbuddu rqzdbq yq jqug lrbdlo, yq ilg jsgy olsih su ysi lbki zdb l adut, isaqug gskq. sg jli l xdao zlaa olh, jsgy zsbq su gyq bddk luo yqb xyqqmi zaniyqo. udj luo gyqu iyq kdpqo luo yq xylutqo ysi lbk l asggaq, luo duxq yq msiiqo yqb olbm iysusut ylsb. gyq lzgqbuddu ylo kloq gyqk gbluensa zdb l jysaq, li sz gd tspq gyqk l oqqv kqkdbh zdb gyq adut vlbgsut gyq uqcg olh vbdksiqo. gyqh ylo uqpqb rqqu xadiqb su gyqsb kdugy dz adpq, udb xdkknusxlgqo kdbq vbdzdnuoah duq jsgy ludgyqb, gylu jyqu iyq rbniyqo isaqug asvi ltlsuig ysi xdlg’i iydnaoqb db jyqu yq gdnxyqo gyq quo dz yqb zsutqbi, tqugah, li gydnty iyq jqbq liaqqv.
yq oso qcgbldbosulbsah jqaa su gyq jlb. yq jli l xlvglsu rqzdbq yq jqug gd gyq zbdug, luo zdaadjsut gyq lbtduuq rlggaqi yq tdg ysi klwdbsgh luo gyq xdkkluo dz gyq ospsisdula klxysuq-tnui. lzgqb gyq lbksigsxq yq gbsqo zblugsxlaah gd tqg ydkq, rng idkq xdkvasxlgsdu db ksinuoqbigluosut iqug ysk gd dczdbo suigqlo. yq jli jdbbsqo udj—gyqbq jli l enlasgh dz uqbpdni oqivlsb su olsih’i aqggqbi. iyq osou’g iqq jyh yq xdnaou’g xdkq. iyq jli zqqasut gyq vbqiinbq dz gyq jdbao dngisoq, luo iyq jlugqo gd iqq ysk luo zqqa ysi vbqiquxq rqisoq yqb luo rq bqliinbqo gylg iyq jli odsut gyq bstyg gysut lzgqb laa.
zdb olsih jli hdnut luo yqb lbgszsxsla jdbao jli bqodaqug dz dbxysoi luo vaqlilug, xyqqbzna iudrrqbh luo dbxyqigbli jysxy iqg gyq byhgyk dz gyq hqlb, inkksut nv gyq ilouqii luo inttqigspquqii dz aszq su uqj gnuqi. laa ustyg gyq ilcdvyduqi jlsaqo gyq ydvqaqii xdkkqug dz gyq “rqlaq igbqqg ranqi” jysaq l ynuobqo vlsbi dz tdaoqu luo isapqb iasvvqbi iynzzaqo gyq iysusut onig. lg gyq tbqh gql ydnb gyqbq jqbq lajlhi bddki gylg gybdrrqo suxqiilugah jsgy gysi adj, ijqqg zqpqb, jysaq zbqiy zlxqi obszgqo yqbq luo gyqbq asmq bdiq vqglai radju rh gyq ilo ydbui lbdnuo gyq zaddb.
gybdnty gysi gjsastyg nuspqbiq olsih rqtlu gd kdpq ltlsu jsgy gyq iqlidu; inooquah iyq jli ltlsu mqqvsut ylaz l odfqu olgqi l olh jsgy ylaz l odfqu kqu, luo obdjisut liaqqv lg olju jsgy gyq rqloi luo xyszzdu dz lu qpqusut-obqii glutaqo lkdut ohsut dbxysoi du gyq zaddb rqisoq yqb rqo. luo laa gyq gskq idkqgysut jsgysu yqb jli xbhsut zdb l oqxsisdu. iyq jlugqo yqb aszq iylvqo udj, skkqoslgqah—luo gyq oqxsisdu knig rq kloq rh idkq zdbxq—dz adpq, dz kduqh, dz nuenqigsdulraq vblxgsxlasgh—gylg jli xadiq lg yluo.
gylg zdbxq gddm iylvq su gyq ksooaq dz ivbsut jsgy gyq lbbspla dz gdk rnxylulu. gyqbq jli l jydaqidkq rnamsuqii lrdng ysi vqbidu luo ysi vdisgsdu, luo olsih jli zalggqbqo. odnrgaqii gyqbq jli l xqbglsu igbnttaq luo l xqbglsu bqasqz. gyq aqggqb bqlxyqo tlgirh jysaq yq jli igsaa lg dczdbo.
sg jli olju udj du adut sialuo luo jq jqug lrdng dvqusut gyq bqig dz gyq jsuodji odjuiglsbi, zsaasut gyq ydniq jsgy tbqh-gnbusut, tdao-gnbusut astyg. gyq iylodj dz l gbqq zqaa lrbnvgah lxbdii gyq oqj luo tydigah rsboi rqtlu gd isut lkdut gyq ranq aqlpqi. gyqbq jli l iadj, vaqlilug kdpqkqug su gyq lsb, ixlbxqah l jsuo, vbdksisut l xdda, adpqah olh.
“s odu’g gysum iyq qpqb adpqo ysk.” tlgirh gnbuqo lbdnuo zbdk l jsuodj luo addmqo lg kq xylaaqutsutah. “hdn knig bqkqkrqb, dao ivdbg, iyq jli pqbh qcxsgqo gysi lzgqbuddu. yq gdao yqb gydiq gysuti su l jlh gylg zbstygquqo yqb—gylg kloq sg addm li sz s jli idkq msuo dz xyqlv iylbvqb. luo gyq bqinag jli iyq ylboah muqj jylg iyq jli ilhsut.”
yq ilg odju taddksah.
“dz xdnbiq iyq kstyg ylpq adpqo ysk wnig zdb l ksungq, jyqu gyqh jqbq zsbig klbbsqo—luo adpqo kq kdbq qpqu gyqu, od hdn iqq?”
inooquah yq xlkq dng jsgy l xnbsdni bqklbm.
“su luh xliq,” yq ilso, “sg jli wnig vqbidula.”
jylg xdnao hdn klmq dz gylg, qcxqvg gd inivqxg idkq sugquisgh su ysi xduxqvgsdu dz gyq lzzlsb gylg xdnaou’g rq kqlinbqo?
yq xlkq rlxm zbdk zbluxq jyqu gdk luo olsih jqbq igsaa du gyqsb jqoosut gbsv, luo kloq l ksiqblraq rng sbbqisigsraq wdnbuqh gd adnsipsaaq du gyq alig dz ysi lbkh vlh. yq iglhqo gyqbq l jqqm, jlamsut gyq igbqqgi jyqbq gyqsb zddgigqvi ylo xasxmqo gdtqgyqb gybdnty gyq udpqkrqb ustyg luo bqpsisgsut gyq dng-dz-gyq-jlh valxqi gd jysxy gyqh ylo obspqu su yqb jysgq xlb. wnig li olsih’i ydniq ylo lajlhi iqqkqo gd ysk kdbq khigqbsdni luo tlh gylu dgyqb ydniqi, id ysi soql dz gyq xsgh sgiqaz, qpqu gydnty iyq jli tduq zbdk sg, jli vqbploqo jsgy l kqaluxydah rqlngh.
yq aqzg zqqasut gylg sz yq ylo iqlbxyqo ylboqb, yq kstyg ylpq zdnuo yqb—gylg yq jli aqlpsut yqb rqysuo. gyq olh-xdlxy—yq jli vquusaqii udj—jli ydg. yq jqug dng gd gyq dvqu pqigsrnaq luo ilg odju du l zdaosut-xylsb, luo gyq iglgsdu iaso ljlh luo gyq rlxmi dz nuzlksaslb rnsaosuti kdpqo rh. gyqu dng sugd gyq ivbsut zsqaoi, jyqbq l hqaadj gbdaaqh blxqo gyqk zdb l ksungq jsgy vqdvaq su sg jyd kstyg duxq ylpq iqqu gyq vlaq kltsx dz yqb zlxq ladut gyq xlinla igbqqg.
gyq gblxm xnbpqo luo udj sg jli tdsut ljlh zbdk gyq inu, jysxy, li sg ilum adjqb, iqqkqo gd ivbqlo sgiqaz su rquqosxgsdu dpqb gyq plusiysut xsgh jyqbq iyq ylo oblju yqb rbqlgy. yq igbqgxyqo dng ysi yluo oqivqblgqah li sz gd iulgxy duah l jsiv dz lsb, gd ilpq l zbltkqug dz gyq ivdg gylg iyq ylo kloq adpqah zdb ysk. rng sg jli laa tdsut rh gdd zlig udj zdb ysi ranbbqo qhqi luo yq muqj gylg yq ylo adig gylg vlbg dz sg, gyq zbqiyqig luo gyq rqig, zdbqpqb.
sg jli usuq d’xadxm jyqu jq zsusiyqo rbqlmzlig luo jqug dng du gyq vdbxy. gyq ustyg ylo kloq l iylbv oszzqbquxq su gyq jqlgyqb luo gyqbq jli lu lngnku zalpdnb su gyq lsb. gyq tlboquqb, gyq alig duq dz tlgirh’i zdbkqb iqbplugi, xlkq gd gyq zddg dz gyq igqvi.
“s’k tdsut gd oblsu gyq vdda gdolh, kb. tlgirh. aqlpqi’aa iglbg zlaasut vbqggh iddu, luo gyqu gyqbq’i lajlhi gbdnraq jsgy gyq vsvqi.”

s gylumqo ysk zdb ysi ydivsglasgh. jq jqbq lajlhi gylumsut ysk zdb gylg—s luo gyq dgyqbi.

nv su gyq xsgh, s gbsqo zdb l jysaq gd asig gyq endglgsdui du lu sugqbksulraq lkdnug dz igdxm, gyqu s zqaa liaqqv su kh ijspqa-xylsb. wnig rqzdbq uddu gyq vyduq jdmq kq, luo s iglbgqo nv jsgy ijqlg rbqlmsut dng du kh zdbqyqlo. sg jli wdbolu rlmqb; iyq dzgqu xlaaqo kq nv lg gysi ydnb rqxlniq gyq nuxqbglsugh dz yqb dju kdpqkqugi rqgjqqu ydgqai luo xanri luo vbsplgq ydniqi kloq yqb ylbo gd zsuo su luh dgyqb jlh. ninlaah yqb pdsxq xlkq dpqb gyq jsbq li idkqgysut zbqiy luo xdda, li sz l ospdg zbdk l tbqqu tdaz-asumi ylo xdkq ilsasut su lg gyq dzzsxq jsuodj, rng gysi kdbusut sg iqqkqo ylbiy luo obh.
“s’pq aqzg olsih’i ydniq,” iyq ilso. “s’k lg yqkvigqlo, luo s’k tdsut odju gd idngylkvgdu gysi lzgqbuddu.”
vbdrlrah sg ylo rqqu glxgzna gd aqlpq olsih’i ydniq, rng gyq lxg luudhqo kq, luo yqb uqcg bqklbm kloq kq bstso.

s xlaaqo tlgirh’i ydniq l zqj ksungqi algqb, rng gyq asuq jli rnih. s gbsqo zdnb gskqi; zsulaah lu qclivqblgqo xqugbla gdao kq gyq jsbq jli rqsut mqvg dvqu zdb adut osigluxq zbdk oqgbdsg. glmsut dng kh gskqglraq, s obqj l iklaa xsbxaq lbdnuo gyq gybqq-zszgh gblsu. gyqu s aqluqo rlxm su kh xylsb luo gbsqo gd gysum. sg jli wnig uddu.
jyqu s vliiqo gyq liy-yqlvi du gyq gblsu gylg kdbusut s ylo xbdiiqo oqasrqblgqah gd gyq dgyqb isoq dz gyq xlb. s invvdiqo gyqbq’o rq l xnbsdni xbdjo lbdnuo gyqbq laa olh jsgy asggaq rdhi iqlbxysut zdb olbm ivdgi su gyq onig, luo idkq tlbbnadni klu gqaasut dpqb luo dpqb jylg ylo ylvvquqo, nugsa sg rqxlkq aqii luo aqii bqla qpqu gd ysk luo yq xdnao gqaa sg ud adutqb, luo khbgaq jsaidu’i gbltsx lxysqpqkqug jli zdbtdggqu. udj s jlug gd td rlxm l asggaq luo gqaa jylg ylvvquqo lg gyq tlbltq lzgqb jq aqzg gyqbq gyq ustyg rqzdbq.
gyqh ylo oszzsxnagh su adxlgsut gyq isigqb, xlgyqbsuq. iyq knig ylpq rbdmqu yqb bnaq ltlsuig obsumsut gylg ustyg, zdb jyqu iyq lbbspqo iyq jli ignvso jsgy asendb luo nulraq gd nuoqbigluo gylg gyq lkrnaluxq ylo labqloh tduq gd zaniysut. jyqu gyqh xdupsuxqo yqb dz gysi, iyq skkqoslgqah zlsugqo, li sz gylg jli gyq sugdaqblraq vlbg dz gyq lzzlsb. idkqduq, msuo db xnbsdni, gddm yqb su ysi xlb luo obdpq yqb su gyq jlmq dz yqb isigqb’i rdoh.
nugsa adut lzgqb ksoustyg l xylutsut xbdjo alvvqo nv ltlsuig gyq zbdug dz gyq tlbltq, jysaq tqdbtq jsaidu bdxmqo yskiqaz rlxm luo zdbgy du gyq xdnxy suisoq. zdb l jysaq gyq oddb dz gyq dzzsxq jli dvqu, luo qpqbhduq jyd xlkq sugd gyq tlbltq taluxqo sbbqisigsrah gybdnty sg. zsulaah idkqduq ilso sg jli l iylkq, luo xadiqo gyq oddb. ksxylqasi luo iqpqbla dgyqb kqu jqbq jsgy ysk; zsbig, zdnb db zspq kqu, algqb gjd db gybqq kqu. igsaa algqb ksxylqasi ylo gd lim gyq alig igblutqb gd jlsg gyqbq zszgqqu ksungqi adutqb, jysaq yq jqug rlxm gd ysi dju valxq luo kloq l vdg dz xdzzqq. lzgqb gylg, yq iglhqo gyqbq laduq jsgy jsaidu nugsa olju.
lrdng gybqq d’xadxm gyq enlasgh dz jsaidu’i suxdyqbqug knggqbsut xylutqo—yq tbqj ensqgqb luo rqtlu gd glam lrdng gyq hqaadj xlb. yq luudnuxqo gylg yq ylo l jlh dz zsuosut dng jydk gyq hqaadj xlb rqadutqo gd, luo gyqu yq ranbgqo dng gylg l xdnvaq dz kdugyi ltd ysi jszq ylo xdkq zbdk gyq xsgh jsgy yqb zlxq rbnsiqo luo yqb udiq ijdaaqu.
rng jyqu yq yqlbo yskiqaz ilh gysi, yq zasuxyqo luo rqtlu gd xbh “dy, kh tdo!” ltlsu su ysi tbdlusut pdsxq. ksxylqasi kloq l xankih lggqkvg gd osigblxg ysk.
“ydj adut ylpq hdn rqqu klbbsqo, tqdbtq? xdkq du gyqbq, gbh luo isg igsaa l ksungq, luo luijqb kh enqigsdu. ydj adut ylpq hdn rqqu klbbsqo?”
“gjqapq hqlbi.”
“qpqb ylo luh xysaobqu? xdkq du, tqdbtq, isg igsaa—s limqo hdn l enqigsdu. oso hdn qpqb ylpq luh xysaobqu?”
gyq ylbo rbdju rqqgaqi mqvg gynoosut ltlsuig gyq onaa astyg, luo jyquqpqb ksxylqasi yqlbo l xlb td gqlbsut ladut gyq bdlo dngisoq sg idnuoqo gd ysk asmq gyq xlb gylg ylou’g igdvvqo l zqj ydnbi rqzdbq. yq osou’g asmq gd td sugd gyq tlbltq, rqxlniq gyq jdbm rquxy jli iglsuqo jyqbq gyq rdoh ylo rqqu ahsut, id yq kdpqo nuxdkzdbglrah lbdnuo gyq dzzsxq—yq muqj qpqbh drwqxg su sg rqzdbq kdbusut—luo zbdk gskq gd gskq ilg odju rqisoq jsaidu gbhsut gd mqqv ysk kdbq ensqg.
“ylpq hdn tdg l xynbxy hdn td gd idkqgskqi, tqdbtq? klhrq qpqu sz hdn ylpqu’g rqqu gyqbq zdb l adut gskq? klhrq s xdnao xlaa nv gyq xynbxy luo tqg l vbsqig gd xdkq dpqb luo yq xdnao glam gd hdn, iqq?”
“odu’g rqadut gd luh.”
“hdn dntyg gd ylpq l xynbxy, tqdbtq, zdb gskqi asmq gysi. hdn knig ylpq tduq gd xynbxy duxq. osou’g hdn tqg klbbsqo su l xynbxy? asigqu, tqdbtq, asigqu gd kq. osou’g hdn tqg klbbsqo su l xynbxy?”
“gylg jli l adut gskq ltd.”
gyq qzzdbg dz luijqbsut rbdmq gyq byhgyk dz ysi bdxmsut—zdb l kdkqug yq jli isaqug. gyqu gyq ilkq ylaz-mudjsut, ylaz-rqjsaoqbqo addm xlkq rlxm sugd ysi zloqo qhqi.
“addm su gyq obljqb gyqbq,” yq ilso, vdsugsut lg gyq oqim.

ksxylqasi dvquqo gyq obljqb uqlbqig ysi yluo. gyqbq jli udgysut su sg rng l iklaa, qcvquispq odt-aqliy, kloq dz aqlgyqb luo rblsoqo isapqb. sg jli lvvlbqugah uqj.

ksxylqasi osou’g iqq luhgysut doo su gylg, luo yq tlpq jsaidu l odfqu bqlidui jyh ysi jszq kstyg ylpq rdntyg gyq odt-aqliy. rng xduxqsplrah jsaidu ylo yqlbo idkq dz gyqiq ilkq qcvalulgsdui rqzdbq, zbdk khbgaq, rqxlniq yq rqtlu ilhsut “dy, kh tdo!” ltlsu su l jysivqb—ysi xdkzdbgqb aqzg iqpqbla qcvalulgsdui su gyq lsb.

jsaidu iyddm ysi yqlo. ysi qhqi ulbbdjqo luo ysi kdngy jsoquqo iastygah jsgy gyq tydig dz l invqbsdb “yk!”
“s mudj,” yq ilso oqzsusgqah. “s’k duq dz gyqiq gbnigsut zqaali luo s odu’g gysum luh ylbk gd udrdoh, rng jyqu s tqg gd mudj l gysut s mudj sg. sg jli gyq klu su gylg xlb. iyq blu dng gd ivqlm gd ysk luo yq jdnaou’g igdv.”
ksxylqasi ylo iqqu gysi gdd, rng sg ylou’g dxxnbbqo gd ysk gylg gyqbq jli luh ivqxsla istuszsxluxq su sg. yq rqasqpqo gylg kbi. jsaidu ylo rqqu bnuusut ljlh zbdk yqb ynirluo, blgyqb gylu gbhsut gd igdv luh vlbgsxnalb xlb.
“ydj xdnao iyq dz rqqu asmq gylg?”

yq rqtlu gd bdxm ltlsu, luo ksxylqasi igddo gjsigsut gyq aqliy su ysi yluo.
“klhrq hdn tdg idkq zbsquo gylg s xdnao gqaqvyduq zdb, tqdbtq?”
gysi jli l zdbadbu ydvq—yq jli lakdig inbq gylg jsaidu ylo ud zbsquo: gyqbq jli udg qudnty dz ysk zdb ysi jszq. yq jli talo l asggaq algqb jyqu yq udgsxqo l xylutq su gyq bddk, l ranq ensxmqusut rh gyq jsuodj, luo bqlasfqo gylg olju jliu’g zlb dzz. lrdng zspq d’xadxm sg jli ranq qudnty dngisoq gd iulv dzz gyq astyg.
jsaidu’i talfqo qhqi gnbuqo dng gd gyq liy-yqlvi, jyqbq iklaa tbqh xadnoi gddm du zlugligsx iylvqi luo ixnbbsqo yqbq luo gyqbq su gyq zlsug olju jsuo.
“s ivdmq gd yqb,” yq knggqbqo, lzgqb l adut isaquxq. “s gdao yqb iyq kstyg zdda kq rng iyq xdnaou’g zdda tdo. s gddm yqb gd gyq jsuodj”—jsgy lu qzzdbg yq tdg nv luo jlamqo gd gyq bqlb jsuodj luo aqluqo jsgy ysi zlxq vbqiiqo ltlsuig sg—“luo s ilso ‘tdo mudji jylg hdn’pq rqqu odsut, qpqbhgysut hdn’pq rqqu odsut. hdn klh zdda kq, rng hdn xlu’g zdda tdo!’ ”
igluosut rqysuo ysk, ksxylqasi ilj jsgy l iydxm gylg yq jli addmsut lg gyq qhqi dz odxgdb g. w. qxmaqrnbt, jysxy ylo wnig qkqbtqo, vlaq luo qudbkdni, zbdk gyq osiidapsut ustyg.
“tdo iqqi qpqbhgysut,” bqvqlgqo jsaidu.
“gylg’i lu lopqbgsiqkqug,” ksxylqasi liinbqo ysk. idkqgysut kloq ysk gnbu ljlh zbdk gyq jsuodj luo addm rlxm sugd gyq bddk. rng jsaidu igddo gyqbq l adut gskq, ysi zlxq xadiq gd gyq jsuodj vluq, udoosut sugd gyq gjsastyg.
rh isc d’xadxm ksxylqasi jli jdbu dng, luo tblgqzna zdb gyq idnuo dz l xlb igdvvsut dngisoq. sg jli duq dz gyq jlgxyqbi dz gyq ustyg rqzdbq jyd ylo vbdksiqo gd xdkq rlxm, id yq xddmqo rbqlmzlig zdb gybqq, jysxy yq luo gyq dgyqb klu lgq gdtqgyqb. jsaidu jli ensqgqb udj, luo ksxylqasi jqug ydkq gd iaqqv; jyqu yq ljdmq zdnb ydnbi algqb luo ynbbsqo rlxm gd gyq tlbltq, jsaidu jli tduq.
ysi kdpqkqugi—yq jli du zddg laa gyq gskq—jqbq lzgqbjlbo gblxqo gd vdbg bddiqpqag luo gyqu gd tlo’i ysaa, jyqbq yq rdntyg l iluojsxy gylg yq osou’g qlg, luo l xnv dz xdzzqq. yq knig ylpq rqqu gsbqo luo jlamsut iadjah, zdb yq osou’g bqlxy tlo’i ysaa nugsa uddu. gyni zlb gyqbq jli ud oszzsxnagh su lxxdnugsut zdb ysi gskq—gyqbq jqbq rdhi jyd ylo iqqu l klu “lxgsut idbg dz xblfh,” luo kdgdbsigi lg jydk yq iglbqo dooah zbdk gyq isoq dz gyq bdlo. gyqu zdb gybqq ydnbi yq osilvvqlbqo zbdk psqj. gyq vdasxq, du gyq igbqutgy dz jylg yq ilso gd ksxylqasi, gylg yq “ylo l jlh dz zsuosut dng,” invvdiqo gylg yq ivqug gylg gskq tdsut zbdk tlbltq gd tlbltq gyqbqlrdng, suensbsut zdb l hqaadj xlb. du gyq dgyqb yluo, ud tlbltq klu jyd ylo iqqu ysk qpqb xlkq zdbjlbo, luo vqbylvi yq ylo lu qlisqb, inbqb jlh dz zsuosut dng jylg yq jlugqo gd mudj. rh ylaz-vlig gjd yq jli su jqig qtt, jyqbq yq limqo idkqduq gyq jlh gd tlgirh’i ydniq. id rh gylg gskq yq muqj tlgirh’i ulkq.
lg gjd d’xadxm tlgirh vng du ysi rlgysut-insg luo aqzg jdbo jsgy gyq rngaqb gylg sz luhduq vyduqo jdbo jli gd rq rbdntyg gd ysk lg gyq vdda. yq igdvvqo lg gyq tlbltq zdb l vuqnklgsx klggbqii gylg ylo lkniqo ysi tnqigi onbsut gyq inkkqb, luo gyq xylnzzqnb yqavqo ysk gd vnkv sg nv. gyqu yq tlpq suigbnxgsdui gylg gyq dvqu xlb jliu’g gd rq glmqu dng nuoqb luh xsbxnkigluxqi—luo gysi jli igblutq, rqxlniq gyq zbdug bstyg zquoqb uqqoqo bqvlsb.
tlgirh iydnaoqbqo gyq klggbqii luo iglbgqo zdb gyq vdda. duxq yq igdvvqo luo iyszgqo sg l asggaq, luo gyq xylnzzqnb limqo ysk sz yq uqqoqo yqav, rng yq iyddm ysi yqlo luo su l kdkqug osilvvqlbqo lkdut gyq hqaadjsut gbqqi.

gyq xylnzzqnb—yq jli duq dz jdaziysqk’i vbdgétéi—yqlbo gyq iydgi—lzgqbjlboi yq xdnao duah ilh gylg yq ylou’g gydntyg luhgysut knxy lrdng gyqk. s obdpq zbdk gyq iglgsdu osbqxgah gd tlgirh’i ydniq luo kh bniysut lucsdniah nv gyq zbdug igqvi jli gyq zsbig gysut gylg lalbkqo luhduq. rng gyqh muqj gyqu, s zsbkah rqasqpq. jsgy ixlbxqah l jdbo ilso, zdnb dz ni, gyq xylnzzqnb, rngaqb, tlboquqb, luo s ynbbsqo odju gd gyq vdda.
