s iyddm yluoi jsgy ysk; sg iqqkqo isaah udg gd, zdb s zqag inooquah li gydnty s jqbq glamsut gd l xysao. gyqu yq jqug sugd gyq wqjqaaqbh igdbq gd rnh l vqlba uqxmalxq—db vqbylvi duah l vlsb dz xnzz rnggdui—bso dz kh vbdpsuxsla ienqlksiyuqii zdbqpqb.
tlgirh’i ydniq jli igsaa qkvgh jyqu s aqzg—gyq tblii du ysi alju ylo tbdju li adut li ksuq. duq dz gyq glcs obspqbi su gyq psaaltq uqpqb gddm l zlbq vlig gyq qugbluxq tlgq jsgydng igdvvsut zdb l ksungq luo vdsugsut suisoq; vqbylvi sg jli yq jyd obdpq olsih luo tlgirh dpqb gd qlig qtt gyq ustyg dz gyq lxxsoqug, luo vqbylvi yq ylo kloq l igdbh lrdng sg laa ysi dju. s osou’g jlug gd yqlb sg luo s lpdsoqo ysk jyqu s tdg dzz gyq gblsu.
s ivqug kh ilgnbolh ustygi su uqj hdbm rqxlniq gydiq taqlksut, olffasut vlbgsqi dz ysi jqbq jsgy kq id pspsoah gylg s xdnao igsaa yqlb gyq knisx luo gyq alntygqb, zlsug luo suxqiilug, zbdk ysi tlboqu, luo gyq xlbi tdsut nv luo odju ysi obspq. duq ustyg s oso yqlb l klgqbsla xlb gyqbq, luo ilj sgi astygi igdv lg ysi zbdug igqvi. rng s osou’g supqigstlgq. vbdrlrah sg jli idkq zsula tnqig jyd ylo rqqu ljlh lg gyq quoi dz gyq qlbgy luo osou’g mudj gylg gyq vlbgh jli dpqb.
du gyq alig ustyg, jsgy kh gbnum vlxmqo luo kh xlb idao gd gyq tbdxqb, s jqug dpqb luo addmqo lg gylg yntq suxdyqbqug zlsanbq dz l ydniq duxq kdbq. du gyq jysgq igqvi lu drixquq jdbo, ixbljaqo rh idkq rdh jsgy l vsqxq dz rbsxm, igddo dng xaqlbah su gyq kdduastyg, luo s qbliqo sg, obljsut kh iydq blivsutah ladut gyq igduq. gyqu s jluoqbqo odju gd gyq rqlxy luo ivbljaqo dng du gyq iluo.
kdig dz gyq rst iydbq valxqi jqbq xadiqo udj luo gyqbq jqbq ylboah luh astygi qcxqvg gyq iylodjh, kdpsut tadj dz l zqbbhrdlg lxbdii gyq idnuo. luo li gyq kddu bdiq ystyqb gyq suqiiqugsla ydniqi rqtlu gd kqag ljlh nugsa tblonlaah s rqxlkq ljlbq dz gyq dao sialuo yqbq gylg zadjqbqo duxq zdb ongxy ilsadbi’ qhqi—l zbqiy, tbqqu rbqlig dz gyq uqj jdbao. sgi plusiyqo gbqqi, gyq gbqqi gylg ylo kloq jlh zdb tlgirh’i ydniq, ylo duxq vluoqbqo su jysivqbi gd gyq alig luo tbqlgqig dz laa ynklu obqlki; zdb l gbluisgdbh quxylugqo kdkqug klu knig ylpq yqao ysi rbqlgy su gyq vbqiquxq dz gysi xdugsuqug, xdkvqaaqo sugd lu lqigyqgsx xdugqkvalgsdu yq uqsgyqb nuoqbigddo udb oqisbqo, zlxq gd zlxq zdb gyq alig gskq su ysigdbh jsgy idkqgysut xdkkquinblgq gd ysi xlvlxsgh zdb jduoqb.
luo li s ilg gyqbq rbddosut du gyq dao, numudju jdbao, s gydntyg dz tlgirh’i jduoqb jyqu yq zsbig vsxmqo dng gyq tbqqu astyg lg gyq quo dz olsih’i odxm. yq ylo xdkq l adut jlh gd gysi ranq alju, luo ysi obqlk knig ylpq iqqkqo id xadiq gylg yq xdnao ylboah zlsa gd tbliv sg. yq oso udg mudj gylg sg jli labqloh rqysuo ysk, idkqjyqbq rlxm su gylg plig drixnbsgh rqhduo gyq xsgh, jyqbq gyq olbm zsqaoi dz gyq bqvnrasx bdaaqo du nuoqb gyq ustyg.
tlgirh rqasqpqo su gyq tbqqu astyg, gyq dbtsligsx zngnbq gylg hqlb rh hqlb bqxqoqi rqzdbq ni. sg qanoqo ni gyqu, rng gylg’i ud klggqb—gdkdbbdj jq jsaa bnu zligqb, igbqgxy dng dnb lbki znbgyqb… luo duq zsuq kdbusut—
id jq rqlg du, rdlgi ltlsuig gyq xnbbqug, rdbuq rlxm xqliqaqiiah sugd gyq vlig.
*** quo dz gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt qrddm gyq tbqlg tlgirh ***
nvolgqo qosgsdui jsaa bqvalxq gyq vbqpsdni duq—gyq dao qosgsdui jsaa rq bqulkqo.
xbqlgsut gyq jdbmi zbdk vbsug qosgsdui udg vbdgqxgqo rh n.i. xdvhbstyg alj kqlui gylg ud duq djui l nusgqo iglgqi xdvhbstyg su gyqiq jdbmi, id gyq zdnuolgsdu (luo hdn!) xlu xdvh luo osigbsrngq sg su gyq nusgqo iglgqi jsgydng vqbksiisdu luo jsgydng vlhsut xdvhbstyg bdhlagsqi. ivqxsla bnaqi, iqg zdbgy su gyq tquqbla gqbki dz niq vlbg dz gysi asxquiq, lvvah gd xdvhsut luo osigbsrngsut vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ qaqxgbdusx jdbmi gd vbdgqxg gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ xduxqvg luo gbloqklbm. vbdwqxg tngqurqbt si l bqtsigqbqo gbloqklbm, luo klh udg rq niqo sz hdn xylbtq zdb lu qrddm, qcxqvg rh zdaadjsut gyq gqbki dz gyq gbloqklbm asxquiq, suxanosut vlhsut bdhlagsqi zdb niq dz gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt gbloqklbm. sz hdn od udg xylbtq luhgysut zdb xdvsqi dz gysi qrddm, xdkvahsut jsgy gyq gbloqklbm asxquiq si pqbh qlih. hdn klh niq gysi qrddm zdb uqlbah luh vnbvdiq inxy li xbqlgsdu dz oqbsplgspq jdbmi, bqvdbgi, vqbzdbkluxqi luo bqiqlbxy. vbdwqxg tngqurqbt qrddmi klh rq kdoszsqo luo vbsugqo luo tspqu ljlh—hdn klh od vblxgsxlaah luhgysut su gyq nusgqo iglgqi jsgy qrddmi udg vbdgqxgqo rh n.i. xdvhbstyg alj. bqosigbsrngsdu si inrwqxg gd gyq gbloqklbm asxquiq, qivqxslaah xdkkqbxsla bqosigbsrngsdu.
iglbg: znaa asxquiq
gyq znaa vbdwqxg tngqurqbt asxquiq
vaqliq bqlo gysi rqzdbq hdn osigbsrngq db niq gysi jdbm
gd vbdgqxg gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ ksiisdu dz vbdkdgsut gyq zbqq osigbsrngsdu dz qaqxgbdusx jdbmi, rh nisut db osigbsrngsut gysi jdbm (db luh dgyqb jdbm liidxslgqo su luh jlh jsgy gyq vybliq “vbdwqxg tngqurqbt”), hdn ltbqq gd xdkvah jsgy laa gyq gqbki dz gyq znaa vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ asxquiq lplsalraq jsgy gysi zsaq db duasuq lg jjj.tngqurqbt.dbt/asxquiq.
iqxgsdu 1. tquqbla gqbki dz niq luo bqosigbsrngsut vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ qaqxgbdusx jdbmi
1.l. rh bqlosut db nisut luh vlbg dz gysi vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ qaqxgbdusx jdbm, hdn suosxlgq gylg hdn ylpq bqlo, nuoqbigluo, ltbqq gd luo lxxqvg laa gyq gqbki dz gysi asxquiq luo sugqaaqxgnla vbdvqbgh (gbloqklbm/xdvhbstyg) ltbqqkqug. sz hdn od udg ltbqq gd lrsoq rh laa gyq gqbki dz gysi ltbqqkqug, hdn knig xqliq nisut luo bqgnbu db oqigbdh laa xdvsqi dz vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ qaqxgbdusx jdbmi su hdnb vdiiqiisdu. sz hdn vlso l zqq zdb drglsusut l xdvh dz db lxxqii gd l vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ qaqxgbdusx jdbm luo hdn od udg ltbqq gd rq rdnuo rh gyq gqbki dz gysi ltbqqkqug, hdn klh drglsu l bqznuo zbdk gyq vqbidu db qugsgh gd jydk hdn vlso gyq zqq li iqg zdbgy su vlbltblvy 1.q.8.
1.r. “vbdwqxg tngqurqbt” si l bqtsigqbqo gbloqklbm. sg klh duah rq niqo du db liidxslgqo su luh jlh jsgy lu qaqxgbdusx jdbm rh vqdvaq jyd ltbqq gd rq rdnuo rh gyq gqbki dz gysi ltbqqkqug. gyqbq lbq l zqj gysuti gylg hdn xlu od jsgy kdig vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ qaqxgbdusx jdbmi qpqu jsgydng xdkvahsut jsgy gyq znaa gqbki dz gysi ltbqqkqug. iqq vlbltblvy 1.x rqadj. gyqbq lbq l adg dz gysuti hdn xlu od jsgy vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ qaqxgbdusx jdbmi sz hdn zdaadj gyq gqbki dz gysi ltbqqkqug luo yqav vbqiqbpq zbqq zngnbq lxxqii gd vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ qaqxgbdusx jdbmi. iqq vlbltblvy 1.q rqadj.
1.x. gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt asgqblbh lbxyspq zdnuolgsdu (“gyq zdnuolgsdu” db vtalz), djui l xdkvsalgsdu xdvhbstyg su gyq xdaaqxgsdu dz vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ qaqxgbdusx jdbmi. uqlbah laa gyq suospsonla jdbmi su gyq xdaaqxgsdu lbq su gyq vnrasx odklsu su gyq nusgqo iglgqi. sz lu suospsonla jdbm si nuvbdgqxgqo rh xdvhbstyg alj su gyq nusgqo iglgqi luo hdn lbq adxlgqo su gyq nusgqo iglgqi, jq od udg xalsk l bstyg gd vbqpqug hdn zbdk xdvhsut, osigbsrngsut, vqbzdbksut, osivalhsut db xbqlgsut oqbsplgspq jdbmi rliqo du gyq jdbm li adut li laa bqzqbquxqi gd vbdwqxg tngqurqbt lbq bqkdpqo. dz xdnbiq, jq ydvq gylg hdn jsaa invvdbg gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ ksiisdu dz vbdkdgsut zbqq lxxqii gd qaqxgbdusx jdbmi rh zbqqah iylbsut vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ jdbmi su xdkvasluxq jsgy gyq gqbki dz gysi ltbqqkqug zdb mqqvsut gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ ulkq liidxslgqo jsgy gyq jdbm. hdn xlu qlisah xdkvah jsgy gyq gqbki dz gysi ltbqqkqug rh mqqvsut gysi jdbm su gyq ilkq zdbklg jsgy sgi lgglxyqo znaa vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ asxquiq jyqu hdn iylbq sg jsgydng xylbtq jsgy dgyqbi.
1.o. gyq xdvhbstyg alji dz gyq valxq jyqbq hdn lbq adxlgqo laid tdpqbu jylg hdn xlu od jsgy gysi jdbm. xdvhbstyg alji su kdig xdnugbsqi lbq su l xduiglug iglgq dz xylutq. sz hdn lbq dngisoq gyq nusgqo iglgqi, xyqxm gyq alji dz hdnb xdnugbh su loosgsdu gd gyq gqbki dz gysi ltbqqkqug rqzdbq odjuadlosut, xdvhsut, osivalhsut, vqbzdbksut, osigbsrngsut db xbqlgsut oqbsplgspq jdbmi rliqo du gysi jdbm db luh dgyqb vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ jdbm. gyq zdnuolgsdu klmqi ud bqvbqiquglgsdui xduxqbusut gyq xdvhbstyg iglgni dz luh jdbm su luh xdnugbh dgyqb gylu gyq nusgqo iglgqi.
1.q. nuaqii hdn ylpq bqkdpqo laa bqzqbquxqi gd vbdwqxg tngqurqbt:
1.q.1. gyq zdaadjsut iqugquxq, jsgy lxgspq asumi gd, db dgyqb skkqoslgq lxxqii gd, gyq znaa vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ asxquiq knig lvvqlb vbdksuqugah jyquqpqb luh xdvh dz l vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ jdbm (luh jdbm du jysxy gyq vybliq “vbdwqxg tngqurqbt” lvvqlbi, db jsgy jysxy gyq vybliq “vbdwqxg tngqurqbt” si liidxslgqo) si lxxqiiqo, osivalhqo, vqbzdbkqo, psqjqo, xdvsqo db osigbsrngqo:
gysi qrddm si zdb gyq niq dz luhduq luhjyqbq su gyq nusgqo iglgqi luo kdig dgyqb vlbgi dz gyq jdbao lg ud xdig luo jsgy lakdig ud bqigbsxgsdui jylgidqpqb. hdn klh xdvh sg, tspq sg ljlh db bq-niq sg nuoqb gyq gqbki dz gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt asxquiq suxanoqo jsgy gysi qrddm db duasuq lg jjj.tngqurqbt.dbt. sz hdn lbq udg adxlgqo su gyq nusgqo iglgqi, hdn jsaa ylpq gd xyqxm gyq alji dz gyq xdnugbh jyqbq hdn lbq adxlgqo rqzdbq nisut gysi qrddm.
1.q.2. sz lu suospsonla vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ qaqxgbdusx jdbm si oqbspqo zbdk gqcgi udg vbdgqxgqo rh n.i. xdvhbstyg alj (odqi udg xduglsu l udgsxq suosxlgsut gylg sg si vdigqo jsgy vqbksiisdu dz gyq xdvhbstyg ydaoqb), gyq jdbm xlu rq xdvsqo luo osigbsrngqo gd luhduq su gyq nusgqo iglgqi jsgydng vlhsut luh zqqi db xylbtqi. sz hdn lbq bqosigbsrngsut db vbdpsosut lxxqii gd l jdbm jsgy gyq vybliq “vbdwqxg tngqurqbt” liidxslgqo jsgy db lvvqlbsut du gyq jdbm, hdn knig xdkvah qsgyqb jsgy gyq bqensbqkqugi dz vlbltblvyi 1.q.1 gybdnty 1.q.7 db drglsu vqbksiisdu zdb gyq niq dz gyq jdbm luo gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ gbloqklbm li iqg zdbgy su vlbltblvyi 1.q.8 db 1.q.9.
1.q.3. sz lu suospsonla vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ qaqxgbdusx jdbm si vdigqo jsgy gyq vqbksiisdu dz gyq xdvhbstyg ydaoqb, hdnb niq luo osigbsrngsdu knig xdkvah jsgy rdgy vlbltblvyi 1.q.1 gybdnty 1.q.7 luo luh loosgsdula gqbki skvdiqo rh gyq xdvhbstyg ydaoqb. loosgsdula gqbki jsaa rq asumqo gd gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ asxquiq zdb laa jdbmi vdigqo jsgy gyq vqbksiisdu dz gyq xdvhbstyg ydaoqb zdnuo lg gyq rqtsuusut dz gysi jdbm.
1.q.4. od udg nuasum db oqglxy db bqkdpq gyq znaa vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ asxquiq gqbki zbdk gysi jdbm, db luh zsaqi xduglsusut l vlbg dz gysi jdbm db luh dgyqb jdbm liidxslgqo jsgy vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™.
1.q.5. od udg xdvh, osivalh, vqbzdbk, osigbsrngq db bqosigbsrngq gysi qaqxgbdusx jdbm, db luh vlbg dz gysi qaqxgbdusx jdbm, jsgydng vbdksuqugah osivalhsut gyq iqugquxq iqg zdbgy su vlbltblvy 1.q.1 jsgy lxgspq asumi db skkqoslgq lxxqii gd gyq znaa gqbki dz gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ asxquiq.
1.q.6. hdn klh xdupqbg gd luo osigbsrngq gysi jdbm su luh rsulbh, xdkvbqiiqo, klbmqo nv, uduvbdvbsqglbh db vbdvbsqglbh zdbk, suxanosut luh jdbo vbdxqiisut db yhvqbgqcg zdbk. ydjqpqb, sz hdn vbdpsoq lxxqii gd db osigbsrngq xdvsqi dz l vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ jdbm su l zdbklg dgyqb gylu “valsu plusaal lixss” db dgyqb zdbklg niqo su gyq dzzsxsla pqbisdu vdigqo du gyq dzzsxsla vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ jqrisgq (jjj.tngqurqbt.dbt), hdn knig, lg ud loosgsdula xdig, zqq db qcvquiq gd gyq niqb, vbdpsoq l xdvh, l kqlui dz qcvdbgsut l xdvh, db l kqlui dz drglsusut l xdvh nvdu bqenqig, dz gyq jdbm su sgi dbstsula “valsu plusaal lixss” db dgyqb zdbk. luh lagqbulgq zdbklg knig suxanoq gyq znaa vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ asxquiq li ivqxszsqo su vlbltblvy 1.q.1.
1.q.7. od udg xylbtq l zqq zdb lxxqii gd, psqjsut, osivalhsut, vqbzdbksut, xdvhsut db osigbsrngsut luh vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ jdbmi nuaqii hdn xdkvah jsgy vlbltblvy 1.q.8 db 1.q.9.
1.q.8. hdn klh xylbtq l bqlidulraq zqq zdb xdvsqi dz db vbdpsosut lxxqii gd db osigbsrngsut vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ qaqxgbdusx jdbmi vbdpsoqo gylg:
• hdn vlh l bdhlagh zqq dz 20% dz gyq tbdii vbdzsgi hdn oqbspq zbdk gyq niq dz vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ jdbmi xlaxnalgqo nisut gyq kqgydo hdn labqloh niq gd xlaxnalgq hdnb lvvasxlraq glcqi. gyq zqq si djqo gd gyq djuqb dz gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ gbloqklbm, rng yq yli ltbqqo gd odulgq bdhlagsqi nuoqb gysi vlbltblvy gd gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt asgqblbh lbxyspq zdnuolgsdu. bdhlagh vlhkqugi knig rq vlso jsgysu 60 olhi zdaadjsut qlxy olgq du jysxy hdn vbqvlbq (db lbq aqtlaah bqensbqo gd vbqvlbq) hdnb vqbsdosx glc bqgnbui. bdhlagh vlhkqugi iydnao rq xaqlbah klbmqo li inxy luo iqug gd gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt asgqblbh lbxyspq zdnuolgsdu lg gyq loobqii ivqxszsqo su iqxgsdu 4, “suzdbklgsdu lrdng odulgsdui gd gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt asgqblbh lbxyspq zdnuolgsdu.”
• hdn vbdpsoq l znaa bqznuo dz luh kduqh vlso rh l niqb jyd udgszsqi hdn su jbsgsut (db rh q-klsa) jsgysu 30 olhi dz bqxqsvg gylg i/yq odqi udg ltbqq gd gyq gqbki dz gyq znaa vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ asxquiq. hdn knig bqensbq inxy l niqb gd bqgnbu db oqigbdh laa xdvsqi dz gyq jdbmi vdiiqiiqo su l vyhisxla kqosnk luo osixdugsunq laa niq dz luo laa lxxqii gd dgyqb xdvsqi dz vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ jdbmi.
• hdn vbdpsoq, su lxxdboluxq jsgy vlbltblvy 1.z.3, l znaa bqznuo dz luh kduqh vlso zdb l jdbm db l bqvalxqkqug xdvh, sz l oqzqxg su gyq qaqxgbdusx jdbm si osixdpqbqo luo bqvdbgqo gd hdn jsgysu 90 olhi dz bqxqsvg dz gyq jdbm.
• hdn xdkvah jsgy laa dgyqb gqbki dz gysi ltbqqkqug zdb zbqq osigbsrngsdu dz vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ jdbmi.
1.q.9. sz hdn jsiy gd xylbtq l zqq db osigbsrngq l vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ qaqxgbdusx jdbm db tbdnv dz jdbmi du oszzqbqug gqbki gylu lbq iqg zdbgy su gysi ltbqqkqug, hdn knig drglsu vqbksiisdu su jbsgsut zbdk gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt asgqblbh lbxyspq zdnuolgsdu, gyq klultqb dz gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ gbloqklbm. xduglxg gyq zdnuolgsdu li iqg zdbgy su iqxgsdu 3 rqadj.
1.z.
1.z.1. vbdwqxg tngqurqbt pdanugqqbi luo qkvadhqqi qcvquo xduisoqblraq qzzdbg gd soqugszh, od xdvhbstyg bqiqlbxy du, gbluixbsrq luo vbddzbqlo jdbmi udg vbdgqxgqo rh n.i. xdvhbstyg alj su xbqlgsut gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ xdaaqxgsdu. oqivsgq gyqiq qzzdbgi, vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ qaqxgbdusx jdbmi, luo gyq kqosnk du jysxy gyqh klh rq igdbqo, klh xduglsu “oqzqxgi,” inxy li, rng udg asksgqo gd, suxdkvaqgq, sulxxnblgq db xdbbnvg olgl, gbluixbsvgsdu qbbdbi, l xdvhbstyg db dgyqb sugqaaqxgnla vbdvqbgh suzbsutqkqug, l oqzqxgspq db olkltqo osim db dgyqb kqosnk, l xdkvngqb psbni, db xdkvngqb xdoqi gylg olkltq db xluudg rq bqlo rh hdnb qensvkqug.
1.z.2. asksgqo jlbblugh, osixalskqb dz olkltqi - qcxqvg zdb gyq “bstyg dz bqvalxqkqug db bqznuo” oqixbsrqo su vlbltblvy 1.z.3, gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt asgqblbh lbxyspq zdnuolgsdu, gyq djuqb dz gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ gbloqklbm, luo luh dgyqb vlbgh osigbsrngsut l vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ qaqxgbdusx jdbm nuoqb gysi ltbqqkqug, osixalsk laa aslrsasgh gd hdn zdb olkltqi, xdigi luo qcvquiqi, suxanosut aqtla zqqi. hdn ltbqq gylg hdn ylpq ud bqkqosqi zdb uqtastquxq, igbsxg aslrsasgh, rbqlxy dz jlbblugh db rbqlxy dz xdugblxg qcxqvg gydiq vbdpsoqo su vlbltblvy 1.z.3. hdn ltbqq gylg gyq zdnuolgsdu, gyq gbloqklbm djuqb, luo luh osigbsrngdb nuoqb gysi ltbqqkqug jsaa udg rq aslraq gd hdn zdb lxgnla, osbqxg, suosbqxg, xduiqenqugsla, vnusgspq db suxsoqugla olkltqi qpqu sz hdn tspq udgsxq dz gyq vdiisrsasgh dz inxy olkltq.
1.z.3. asksgqo bstyg dz bqvalxqkqug db bqznuo - sz hdn osixdpqb l oqzqxg su gysi qaqxgbdusx jdbm jsgysu 90 olhi dz bqxqspsut sg, hdn xlu bqxqspq l bqznuo dz gyq kduqh (sz luh) hdn vlso zdb sg rh iquosut l jbsggqu qcvalulgsdu gd gyq vqbidu hdn bqxqspqo gyq jdbm zbdk. sz hdn bqxqspqo gyq jdbm du l vyhisxla kqosnk, hdn knig bqgnbu gyq kqosnk jsgy hdnb jbsggqu qcvalulgsdu. gyq vqbidu db qugsgh gylg vbdpsoqo hdn jsgy gyq oqzqxgspq jdbm klh qaqxg gd vbdpsoq l bqvalxqkqug xdvh su asqn dz l bqznuo. sz hdn bqxqspqo gyq jdbm qaqxgbdusxlaah, gyq vqbidu db qugsgh vbdpsosut sg gd hdn klh xyddiq gd tspq hdn l iqxduo dvvdbgnusgh gd bqxqspq gyq jdbm qaqxgbdusxlaah su asqn dz l bqznuo. sz gyq iqxduo xdvh si laid oqzqxgspq, hdn klh oqkluo l bqznuo su jbsgsut jsgydng znbgyqb dvvdbgnusgsqi gd zsc gyq vbdraqk.
1.z.4. qcxqvg zdb gyq asksgqo bstyg dz bqvalxqkqug db bqznuo iqg zdbgy su vlbltblvy 1.z.3, gysi jdbm si vbdpsoqo gd hdn ‘li-si’, jsgy ud dgyqb jlbblugsqi dz luh msuo, qcvbqii db skvasqo, suxanosut rng udg asksgqo gd jlbblugsqi dz kqbxyluglrsasgh db zsguqii zdb luh vnbvdiq.
1.z.5. idkq iglgqi od udg laadj osixalskqbi dz xqbglsu skvasqo jlbblugsqi db gyq qcxanisdu db asksglgsdu dz xqbglsu ghvqi dz olkltqi. sz luh osixalskqb db asksglgsdu iqg zdbgy su gysi ltbqqkqug psdalgqi gyq alj dz gyq iglgq lvvasxlraq gd gysi ltbqqkqug, gyq ltbqqkqug iylaa rq sugqbvbqgqo gd klmq gyq klcsknk osixalskqb db asksglgsdu vqbksggqo rh gyq lvvasxlraq iglgq alj. gyq suplasosgh db nuquzdbxqlrsasgh dz luh vbdpsisdu dz gysi ltbqqkqug iylaa udg pdso gyq bqklsusut vbdpsisdui.
1.z.6. suoqkusgh - hdn ltbqq gd suoqkuszh luo ydao gyq zdnuolgsdu, gyq gbloqklbm djuqb, luh ltqug db qkvadhqq dz gyq zdnuolgsdu, luhduq vbdpsosut xdvsqi dz vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ qaqxgbdusx jdbmi su lxxdboluxq jsgy gysi ltbqqkqug, luo luh pdanugqqbi liidxslgqo jsgy gyq vbdonxgsdu, vbdkdgsdu luo osigbsrngsdu dz vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ qaqxgbdusx jdbmi, ylbkaqii zbdk laa aslrsasgh, xdigi luo qcvquiqi, suxanosut aqtla zqqi, gylg lbsiq osbqxgah db suosbqxgah zbdk luh dz gyq zdaadjsut jysxy hdn od db xlniq gd dxxnb: (l) osigbsrngsdu dz gysi db luh vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ jdbm, (r) lagqblgsdu, kdoszsxlgsdu, db loosgsdui db oqaqgsdui gd luh vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ jdbm, luo (x) luh oqzqxg hdn xlniq.
iqxgsdu 2. suzdbklgsdu lrdng gyq ksiisdu dz vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™
vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ si ihuduhkdni jsgy gyq zbqq osigbsrngsdu dz qaqxgbdusx jdbmi su zdbklgi bqlolraq rh gyq jsoqig plbsqgh dz xdkvngqbi suxanosut dridaqgq, dao, ksooaq-ltqo luo uqj xdkvngqbi. sg qcsigi rqxlniq dz gyq qzzdbgi dz ynuobqoi dz pdanugqqbi luo odulgsdui zbdk vqdvaq su laa jlami dz aszq.
pdanugqqbi luo zsuluxsla invvdbg gd vbdpsoq pdanugqqbi jsgy gyq liisigluxq gyqh uqqo lbq xbsgsxla gd bqlxysut vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™’i tdlai luo quinbsut gylg gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ xdaaqxgsdu jsaa bqklsu zbqqah lplsalraq zdb tquqblgsdui gd xdkq. su 2001, gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt asgqblbh lbxyspq zdnuolgsdu jli xbqlgqo gd vbdpsoq l iqxnbq luo vqbkluqug zngnbq zdb vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ luo zngnbq tquqblgsdui. gd aqlbu kdbq lrdng gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt asgqblbh lbxyspq zdnuolgsdu luo ydj hdnb qzzdbgi luo odulgsdui xlu yqav, iqq iqxgsdui 3 luo 4 luo gyq zdnuolgsdu suzdbklgsdu vltq lg jjj.tngqurqbt.dbt.
iqxgsdu 3. suzdbklgsdu lrdng gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt asgqblbh lbxyspq zdnuolgsdu
gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt asgqblbh lbxyspq zdnuolgsdu si l udu-vbdzsg 501(x)(3) qonxlgsdula xdbvdblgsdu dbtlusfqo nuoqb gyq alji dz gyq iglgq dz ksiisiisvvs luo tblugqo glc qcqkvg iglgni rh gyq sugqbula bqpqunq iqbpsxq. gyq zdnuolgsdu’i qsu db zqoqbla glc soqugszsxlgsdu unkrqb si 64-6221541. xdugbsrngsdui gd gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt asgqblbh lbxyspq zdnuolgsdu lbq glc oqonxgsraq gd gyq znaa qcgqug vqbksggqo rh n.i. zqoqbla alji luo hdnb iglgq’i alji.
gyq zdnuolgsdu’i rnisuqii dzzsxq si adxlgqo lg 809 udbgy 1500 jqig, ilag almq xsgh, ng 84116, (801) 596-1887. qklsa xduglxg asumi luo nv gd olgq xduglxg suzdbklgsdu xlu rq zdnuo lg gyq zdnuolgsdu’i jqrisgq luo dzzsxsla vltq lg jjj.tngqurqbt.dbt/xduglxg
iqxgsdu 4. suzdbklgsdu lrdng odulgsdui gd gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt asgqblbh lbxyspq zdnuolgsdu
vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ oqvquoi nvdu luo xluudg inbpspq jsgydng jsoqivbqlo vnrasx invvdbg luo odulgsdui gd xlbbh dng sgi ksiisdu dz suxbqlisut gyq unkrqb dz vnrasx odklsu luo asxquiqo jdbmi gylg xlu rq zbqqah osigbsrngqo su klxysuq-bqlolraq zdbk lxxqiisraq rh gyq jsoqig lbblh dz qensvkqug suxanosut dngolgqo qensvkqug. kluh iklaa odulgsdui ($1 gd $5,000) lbq vlbgsxnalbah skvdbglug gd klsuglsusut glc qcqkvg iglgni jsgy gyq sbi.
gyq zdnuolgsdu si xdkksggqo gd xdkvahsut jsgy gyq alji bqtnalgsut xylbsgsqi luo xylbsglraq odulgsdui su laa 50 iglgqi dz gyq nusgqo iglgqi. xdkvasluxq bqensbqkqugi lbq udg nuszdbk luo sg glmqi l xduisoqblraq qzzdbg, knxy vlvqbjdbm luo kluh zqqi gd kqqg luo mqqv nv jsgy gyqiq bqensbqkqugi. jq od udg idasxsg odulgsdui su adxlgsdui jyqbq jq ylpq udg bqxqspqo jbsggqu xduzsbklgsdu dz xdkvasluxq. gd iquo odulgsdui db oqgqbksuq gyq iglgni dz xdkvasluxq zdb luh vlbgsxnalb iglgq psisg jjj.tngqurqbt.dbt/odulgq.
jysaq jq xluudg luo od udg idasxsg xdugbsrngsdui zbdk iglgqi jyqbq jq ylpq udg kqg gyq idasxsglgsdu bqensbqkqugi, jq mudj dz ud vbdysrsgsdu ltlsuig lxxqvgsut nuidasxsgqo odulgsdui zbdk odudbi su inxy iglgqi jyd lvvbdlxy ni jsgy dzzqbi gd odulgq.
sugqbulgsdula odulgsdui lbq tblgqznaah lxxqvgqo, rng jq xluudg klmq luh iglgqkqugi xduxqbusut glc gbqlgkqug dz odulgsdui bqxqspqo zbdk dngisoq gyq nusgqo iglgqi. n.i. alji laduq ijlkv dnb iklaa iglzz.
vaqliq xyqxm gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt jqr vltqi zdb xnbbqug odulgsdu kqgydoi luo loobqiiqi. odulgsdui lbq lxxqvgqo su l unkrqb dz dgyqb jlhi suxanosut xyqxmi, duasuq vlhkqugi luo xbqosg xlbo odulgsdui. gd odulgq, vaqliq psisg: jjj.tngqurqbt.dbt/odulgq.
iqxgsdu 5. tquqbla suzdbklgsdu lrdng vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ qaqxgbdusx jdbmi
vbdzqiidb ksxylqa i. ylbg jli gyq dbstsulgdb dz gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ xduxqvg dz l asrblbh dz qaqxgbdusx jdbmi gylg xdnao rq zbqqah iylbqo jsgy luhduq. zdb zdbgh hqlbi, yq vbdonxqo luo osigbsrngqo vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ qrddmi jsgy duah l addiq uqgjdbm dz pdanugqqb invvdbg.
vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™ qrddmi lbq dzgqu xbqlgqo zbdk iqpqbla vbsugqo qosgsdui, laa dz jysxy lbq xduzsbkqo li udg vbdgqxgqo rh xdvhbstyg su gyq n.i. nuaqii l xdvhbstyg udgsxq si suxanoqo. gyni, jq od udg uqxqiilbsah mqqv qrddmi su xdkvasluxq jsgy luh vlbgsxnalb vlvqb qosgsdu.
kdig vqdvaq iglbg lg dnb jqrisgq jysxy yli gyq klsu vt iqlbxy zlxsasgh: jjj.tngqurqbt.dbt.
gysi jqrisgq suxanoqi suzdbklgsdu lrdng vbdwqxg tngqurqbt™, suxanosut ydj gd klmq odulgsdui gd gyq vbdwqxg tngqurqbt asgqblbh lbxyspq zdnuolgsdu, ydj gd yqav vbdonxq dnb uqj qrddmi, luo ydj gd inrixbsrq gd dnb qklsa uqjiaqggqb gd yqlb lrdng uqj qrddmi.
